##### **MODF-SIR: A Multi-agent Omni-modal Distilled Framework for Social Intelligence Reasoning**
2606.12018v1 by Shang Ma, Jisheng Dang, Wencan Zhang, Yifan Zhang, Bimei Wang, Hong Peng, Bin Hu, Qi Tian, Tat-Seng Chua

We propose a multi-agent collaborative framework built upon a lightweight Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM), specifically designed for social intelligence reasoning. A key feature of our approach is that both the training and inference phases are augmented via knowledge distillation. Within this architecture, multi-modal data pertinent to social intelligence is precisely localized. Furthermore, relevant long-tail events are identified, extracted, and rendered as formatted, explicit text. This formatting strategy prevents critical long-tail information from being overshadowed by head events and environmental noise during the tokenization process. Specifically, we integrate Test-Time Adaptation (TTA) across the entire reasoning pipeline, encompassing the extraction and representation of long-tail events, Chain-of-Thought (CoT) prompting, and self-reflection. This TTA mechanism is also distillation-enhanced, utilizing Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) to fine-tune the foundation model exclusively for instance-level reasoning. Extensive evaluations against various open-source and proprietary AI models across multiple benchmarks demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework. With around 30% of training data from IntentTrain, we achieve state-of-the-art results. Codes are available at https://github.com/eeee-sys/MODF-SIR, demo is available at https://huggingface.co/spaces/Harry-1234/MODF-SIR, LoRA is available at https://huggingface.co/Harry-1234/MODF-SIR and the dataset for training router is available at https://huggingface.co/datasets/Harry-1234/IntentRouterTrain.

摘要：我們提出了一個基於輕量級多模態大型語言模型（MLLM）的多代理協作框架，專門設計用於社會智能推理。我們方法的一個關鍵特徵是訓練和推理階段都通過知識蒸餾進行增強。在這個架構中，與社會智能相關的多模態數據被精確定位。此外，相關的長尾事件被識別、提取並呈現為格式化的明確文本。這種格式化策略防止了關鍵的長尾信息在標記過程中被頭事件和環境噪音所掩蓋。具體而言，我們在整個推理流程中整合了測試時適應（TTA），涵蓋了長尾事件的提取和表示、思維鏈（CoT）提示以及自我反思。這一TTA機制也得到了蒸餾增強，利用低秩適應（LoRA）專門對基礎模型進行微調以實現實例級推理。對各種開源和專有AI模型在多個基準上的廣泛評估顯示了所提框架的有效性。通過約30%的來自IntentTrain的訓練數據，我們實現了最先進的結果。代碼可在 https://github.com/eeee-sys/MODF-SIR 獲得，演示可在 https://huggingface.co/spaces/Harry-1234/MODF-SIR 獲得，LoRA可在 https://huggingface.co/Harry-1234/MODF-SIR 獲得，訓練路由器的數據集可在 https://huggingface.co/datasets/Harry-1234/IntentRouterTrain 獲得。

##### **The Art of Interrogation: Consistency Amplifies Factuality in Spatial Reasoning**
2606.11918v1 by Theo Uscidda, Marta Tintore Gazulla, Maks Ovsjanikov, Federico Tombari, Leonidas Guibas

Current Large Reasoning Models (LRMs) exhibit remarkable general capabilities but significantly underperform in spatial reasoning tasks. Existing approaches treat this gap as a knowledge deficit, relying on supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to ingest labeled spatial data from external vision sources or synthetic engines. In contrast, we argue that for many tasks, spatial reasoning capabilities are already present in pre-trained LRMs but require alignment through logical coherence under geometric 2D and 3D constraints. In this work, we propose a self-supervised reinforcement learning (RL) framework that targets the internal reasoning process without requiring ground-truth annotations. By formalizing the notion of consistency verifiers -- reward functions that check for geometric and semantic consistency under transformations -- we demonstrate that models can improve their spatial reasoning abilities. We use both image transformations, like flipping, and textual transformations, like swapping the order of objects in the question, and propose a new optimal transport-based RL strategy, OT-GRPO, which is a minimal-matching variant of group relative policy optimization tailored to pairwise verifiers. We show that this label-free consistency training approaches the accuracy of models trained with ground-truth supervision and achieves similar generalization across diverse tasks and data domains.

摘要：目前的大型推理模型（LRMs）展現出卓越的通用能力，但在空間推理任務中表現顯著不足。現有的方法將這一差距視為知識缺失，依賴於監督式微調（SFT）來從外部視覺來源或合成引擎中攝取標記的空間數據。相反，我們主張對於許多任務，空間推理能力已經存在於預訓練的LRMs中，但需要通過幾何2D和3D約束下的邏輯一致性來進行對齊。在這項工作中，我們提出了一個自我監督的強化學習（RL）框架，旨在針對內部推理過程，而不需要真實標註。通過形式化一致性驗證器的概念——檢查在變換下幾何和語義一致性的獎勵函數——我們展示了模型可以提高其空間推理能力。我們使用了圖像變換，如翻轉，以及文本變換，如在問題中交換物體的順序，並提出了一種基於最優運輸的RL策略OT-GRPO，這是一種針對成對驗證器的最小匹配變體的群體相對政策優化。我們顯示這種無標籤的一致性訓練接近於使用真實監督訓練的模型的準確性，並在不同任務和數據領域中達到了類似的泛化能力。

##### **GraspLLM: Towards Zero-Shot Generalization on Text-Attributed Graphs with LLMs**
2606.11898v2 by Hengyi Feng, Zeang Sheng, Meiyi Qiang, Yang Li, Wentao Zhang

Research on Text-Attributed Graphs (TAGs) has gained significant attention recently due to its broad applications across various real-world data scenarios, such as citation networks, e-commerce platforms, social media, and web pages. Inspired by the remarkable semantic understanding ability of Large Language Models (LLMs), there have been numerous attempts to integrate LLMs into TAGs. However, existing methods still struggle to generalize across diverse graphs and tasks, and their ability to capture transferable graph structural patterns remains limited. To address this, we introduce the GraspLLM, a framework that combines Graph structural comprehension with semantic understanding prowess of LLMs to enhance the cross-dataset and cross-task generalizability. Specifically, we represent node texts from different graphs in a unified semantic space with a frozen general embedding model, on top of which we perform motif-aware contrastive learning across multiple motif-induced adjacency matrices to extract dataset-agnostic structural information. Then, with our proposed optimal contextual subgraph, we extract the most contextually relevant subgraph for each target node and align these subgraphs to the token space of LLM via an alignment projector. Extensive experiments on TAG benchmark datasets spanning diverse domains reveal that GraspLLM consistently outperforms previous LLM-based methods for TAGs, especially in zero-shot scenarios, highlighting its strong generalizability across different datasets and tasks. Our code is available at https://github.com/Heinz217/GraspLLM.

摘要：研究文本屬性圖 (TAGs) 最近因其在各種現實世界數據場景中的廣泛應用而受到極大關注，例如引用網絡、電子商務平台、社交媒體和網頁。受到大型語言模型 (LLMs) 卓越的語義理解能力啟發，已有許多嘗試將 LLMs 整合到 TAGs 中。然而，現有方法在不同圖形和任務之間的泛化能力仍然存在困難，並且它們捕捉可轉移圖形結構模式的能力仍然有限。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了 GraspLLM，一個將圖形結構理解與 LLM 的語義理解能力相結合的框架，以增強跨數據集和跨任務的泛化能力。具體而言，我們使用一個凍結的通用嵌入模型，將來自不同圖形的節點文本表示為統一的語義空間，在此基礎上，我們在多個由主題誘導的鄰接矩陣上進行主題感知對比學習，以提取與數據集無關的結構信息。然後，通過我們提出的最佳上下文子圖，我們為每個目標節點提取最具上下文相關性的子圖，並通過對齊投影器將這些子圖對齊到 LLM 的標記空間。對跨越不同領域的 TAG 基準數據集進行的廣泛實驗顯示，GraspLLM 在 TAGs 的 LLM 基礎方法中始終表現優於之前的方法，特別是在零樣本場景中，突顯了其在不同數據集和任務中的強泛化能力。我們的代碼可在 https://github.com/Heinz217/GraspLLM 獲得。

##### **Fine-tuning Multi-modal LLMs with ART: Art-based Reinforcement Training**
2606.11854v1 by Michal Chudoba, Sergey Alyaev, Petra Galuscakova, Tomasz Wiktorski

There are two main Parameter-Efficient Fine-Tuning (PEFT) techniques for Large Language Models (LLMs). While Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) introduces additional weights between the LLM layers, Soft Prompting introduces additional fine-tuning-specific raw tokens to an LLM input. However, both require modification to the computational graphs of precompiled, preoptimized LLMs. As a result, neither is fully supported in high-throughput engines like vLLM. We propose fine-tuning with ART (Art-based Reinforcement Training). The method injects information into a frozen Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM) by optimizing only its raw visual input, thus enabling the soft-token approach on pre-compiled computational graphs. It relies on backpropagation of gradients back into a plain pixel array and thus supports any fine-tuning objective. Moreover, the optimized visual input can be stylized as task-relevant computational artworks. The approach's effectiveness is confirmed for different sizes of a popular open Qwen architecture and for several textual benchmarks. Specifically, ART reaches accuracy competitive with LoRA across mathematics and structured-tool-use benchmarks.

摘要：有兩種主要的參數高效微調（PEFT）技術用於大型語言模型（LLMs）。低秩適應（LoRA）在LLM層之間引入額外的權重，而軟提示則在LLM輸入中引入額外的微調專用原始標記。然而，兩者都需要對預編譯、預優化的LLM的計算圖進行修改。因此，這兩者在高吞吐量引擎如vLLM中都不完全受支持。我們提出使用ART（基於藝術的增強訓練）進行微調。該方法通過僅優化其原始視覺輸入，將信息注入到一個凍結的多模態大型語言模型（MLLM）中，從而在預編譯的計算圖上啟用軟標記方法。它依賴於將梯度反向傳播回普通像素數組，因此支持任何微調目標。此外，優化的視覺輸入可以被風格化為與任務相關的計算藝術作品。該方法的有效性在不同大小的流行開放Qwen架構和幾個文本基準上得到了證實。具體而言，ART在數學和結構化工具使用基準上達到了與LoRA相競爭的準確性。

##### **Task-Aware Structured Memory for Dynamic Multi-modal In-Context Learning**
2606.11853v1 by Zhirui Chen, Ziwei Chen, Ling Shao

Multi-modal large language models (MLLMs) depend on in-context learning (ICL) for rapid task adaptation, but their scalability is severely limited by finite context windows and the growing cost of key-value (KV) caches in long multi-modal sequences. Existing memory compression approaches typically rely on rigid token removal or sample-dependent importance estimation, which introduces bias, disrupts semantic structure, particularly for visual representations, and yields static memories that cannot adapt to new queries. We introduce TASM (Task-Aware Structured Memory), a training-free framework that addresses these limitations through task-aware, structure-preserving, and dynamically accessible memory construction. TASM employs task-vector guided compression to replace sample-specific signals with a task-level direction that captures shared relevance across demonstrations. To preserve the underlying manifold, it applies semantics-aware token merging via bipartite graph matching, aggregating tokens without destructive pruning. Finally, TASM structures memory into a hierarchy comprising a compact Core Memory and a Latent Bank, facilitating query-adaptive dynamic retrieval. Evaluations confirm TASM maintains high performance under heavy compression, effectively balancing efficiency with adaptability.

摘要：多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）依賴於上下文學習（ICL）以快速適應任務，但其可擴展性受到有限上下文窗口和長多模態序列中鍵值（KV）快取日益增長的成本的嚴重限制。現有的記憶壓縮方法通常依賴於僵化的標記移除或樣本依賴的重要性估計，這引入了偏差，破壞了語義結構，特別是對於視覺表示，並產生無法適應新查詢的靜態記憶。我們引入了 TASM（任務感知結構記憶），這是一個無需訓練的框架，通過任務感知、結構保留和動態可訪問的記憶構建來解決這些限制。TASM 採用任務向量引導壓縮，將樣本特定信號替換為捕捉跨示範共享相關性的任務級方向。為了保留底層流形，它通過二分圖匹配應用語義感知的標記合併，聚合標記而不進行破壞性修剪。最後，TASM 將記憶結構化為一個層次，包含一個緊湊的核心記憶和一個潛在庫，促進查詢自適應的動態檢索。評估結果確認 TASM 在重度壓縮下保持高性能，有效平衡了效率與適應性。

##### **From Uniform to Learned Graph Priors: Diffusion for Structure Discovery**
2606.11831v1 by Qi Shao, Hao Guo, Jiawen Chen, Duxin Chen, Wenwu Yu

Neural relational inference (NRI) methods discover interaction graphs from trajectories through variational reasoning on discrete potential edges. However, these methods typically rely on oversimplified, factorized graph priors. Such priors, typically nearing uniform distributions, treat edges as independent entities. This systemic misalignment does not match the real-world systems and yields diffuse and indecisive edge posteriors limiting the reliability of structural discovery. To address this, we propose \textit{Diff-prior}, a diffusion-parameterized adaptive prior used to calibrate latent graph distribution rather than generate graphs. Our core insight is to reframe prior integration as a learnable denoising-style calibration that organizes scattered, uncertain edge posteriors into a more reliable overall structure which can be trained by the diffusion model. Diff-prior learns an adaptive structure prior that performs structured calibration on the edge posteriors during inference, guiding it towards a distribution closer to the underlying structure. The diff-prior operates before structural sampling and acts as a denoising calibrator directly on the encoder edge distribution, which provides a generic training paradigm over structured variables. Experiments on standard benchmarks validated our framework, and the results indicate that Diff-prior improves the performance of structure inference and generates more decisive edge posteriors across multiple NRI-family architectures. The code is available on https://github.com/Hardy158118/Diffprior.

摘要：神經關係推斷（NRI）方法透過對離散潛在邊的變分推理從軌跡中發現互動圖。<lb/>然而，這些方法通常依賴於過於簡化的因子化圖先驗。<lb/>這些先驗通常接近均勻分佈，將邊視為獨立的實體。<lb/>這種系統性的錯位與現實世界系統不符，產生擴散且不確定的邊後驗，限制了結構發現的可靠性。<lb/>為了解決這個問題，我們提出了\textit{Diff-prior}，這是一種擴散參數化的自適應先驗，用於校準潛在圖分佈，而不是生成圖。<lb/>我們的核心見解是將先驗整合重新框架為可學習的去噪風格校準，將分散的不確定邊後驗組織成更可靠的整體結構，這可以通過擴散模型進行訓練。<lb/>Diff-prior學習一種自適應結構先驗，在推理過程中對邊後驗進行結構化校準，引導其朝向更接近潛在結構的分佈。<lb/>Diff-prior在結構採樣之前運作，並作為直接對編碼器邊分佈進行去噪校準的工具，這提供了一種針對結構變量的通用訓練範式。<lb/>在標準基準上的實驗驗證了我們的框架，結果表明Diff-prior提高了結構推斷的性能，並在多個NRI家族架構中生成了更具決斷性的邊後驗。<lb/>代碼可在https://github.com/Hardy158118/Diffprior上獲得。

##### **WorldReasoner: Evaluating Whether Language Model Agents Forecast Events with Valid Reasoning**
2606.11816v1 by Yizhou Chi, Eric Chamoun, Zifeng Ding, Andreas Vlachos

Forecasting real-world events requires language-model agents to reason under uncertainty from incomplete, time-bounded information. Yet evaluating whether agents genuinely forecast requires more than final-answer accuracy: a model may be correct by recalling memorized training facts, citing fabricated evidence, or producing an unsupported causal story. We present WorldReasoner, an evaluation framework for temporally valid event forecasting. Each task gives an agent a resolved forecasting question, a simulated forecast date, and access only to evidence available before that date; after resolution, the framework scores the submitted probability, cited evidence, and optional causal event graph. WorldReasoner reports three complementary axes: outcome quality against resolved answers, evidence quality over cited sources, and reasoning quality against post-resolution hindsight graphs. The benchmark is built by an agentic construction pipeline that generates forecasting questions, collects time-stamped evidence, and builds hindsight reference graphs at scale, yielding 345 resolved tasks derived from 14,141 articles with graphs covering 8,087 extracted events. Across six controlled agent settings, temporally valid retrieval is the strongest driver of outcome accuracy; causal graph construction improves key-event recovery; and correct graph-enabled forecasts are more strongly grounded in key events and relevant sources, yet agents still struggle to convert grounded evidence into calibrated probabilities.

摘要：預測真實世界事件需要語言模型代理在不確定性下從不完整的、時間有限的信息中進行推理。<lb/>然而，評估代理是否真正進行預測需要的不僅僅是最終答案的準確性：一個模型可能通過回憶記憶中的訓練事實、引用虛構的證據或產生不支持的因果故事來正確。<lb/>我們提出了WorldReasoner，一個用於時間有效事件預測的評估框架。<lb/>每個任務為代理提供一個解決的預測問題、一個模擬的預測日期，以及僅能訪問在該日期之前可用的證據；在解決後，該框架評分提交的概率、引用的證據和可選的因果事件圖。<lb/>WorldReasoner報告三個互補的軸心：針對解決答案的結果質量、針對引用來源的證據質量，以及針對解決後的回顧圖的推理質量。<lb/>該基準是通過一個代理建構管道建立的，該管道生成預測問題、收集時間戳證據，並大規模構建回顧參考圖，產生了345個來自14,141篇文章的解決任務，這些圖涵蓋了8,087個提取的事件。<lb/>在六個受控的代理設置中，時間有效的檢索是結果準確性的最強驅動因素；因果圖的構建改善了關鍵事件的恢復；並且正確的圖形啟用預測更強烈地基於關鍵事件和相關來源，但代理仍然難以將基於證據的內容轉化為經過校準的概率。

##### **Fast Speech Foundation Model Distillation Using Interleaved Stacking**
2606.11766v1 by Eungbeom Kim, Kyogu Lee

Distilling a large speech foundation model (SFM) into an efficient student model has been successfully applied to low-resource environments. Although distillation reduces inference latency, it requires an additional student model training. However, the training efficiency of SFM distillation remains underexplored. In this work, we explore training acceleration of SFM distillation to speed up model deployment. We examine the potential of stacking, in which the model depth is progressively increased through training until the target model depth is reached. While existing stacking methods improve training speed, they suffer from performance degradation. To handle this limitation, we propose interleaved stacking, a novel stacking method that consistently preserves layer position throughout the stacking process. This property is particularly critical in SFMs, in which each layer encodes distinct layer-specific knowledge. We validate the effectiveness of the proposed method on SUPERB.

摘要：將大型語音基礎模型（SFM）蒸餾成高效的學生模型已成功應用於資源有限的環境中。<lb/>儘管蒸餾減少了推理延遲，但它需要額外的學生模型訓練。<lb/>然而，SFM蒸餾的訓練效率仍然未被充分探索。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們探索了SFM蒸餾的訓練加速，以加快模型部署。<lb/>我們檢視了堆疊的潛力，其中模型深度透過訓練逐步增加，直到達到目標模型深度。<lb/>雖然現有的堆疊方法提高了訓練速度，但它們遭遇了性能下降的問題。<lb/>為了解決這一限制，我們提出了交錯堆疊，一種新穎的堆疊方法，該方法在整個堆疊過程中始終保持層位置。<lb/>這一特性在SFM中尤為關鍵，因為每一層編碼了獨特的層特定知識。<lb/>我們在SUPERB上驗證了所提方法的有效性。

##### **From Prompts to Tokens: Internalizing Causal Supervision in Vision-Language Model for Multi-Image Causal Reasoning**
2606.11745v1 by Haoping Yu, Yuanxi Li, Jing Ma

Visual causal reasoning is essential for understanding and intervening in the physical world, requiring identification of causal variables from visual inputs and reasoning over intervention effects. Despite recent progress, large vision--language models (VLMs) remain brittle at such tasks, especially for interventional and counterfactual queries over multi-image inputs. Most existing explorations inject causal knowledge via textual prompts, leaving causal mechanisms external to model execution and limiting reliable control during inference. To address this problem, we propose BridgeVLM, which internalizes visual causal reasoning by inducing a causal graph from multi-image inputs and converting it into structured Causal Tokens executed by RAMP layers injected into the LLM decoder for causal message passing. We further introduce a unified training interface M3S for fine-grained causal supervision from different granularities (local/global level). BridgeVLM achieves 54.4% accuracy on intervention tasks on CausalVLBench (vs. 33.2% with prompt-level supervision), improves results on Causal3D from 43.6% to 49.0%, and substantially improves causal structure learning on CausalVLBench ($F_1$: 33.4% $\rightarrow$ 75.1%).

摘要：視覺因果推理對於理解和介入物理世界至關重要，這需要從視覺輸入中識別因果變量並推理介入效果。儘管最近取得了一些進展，但大型視覺-語言模型（VLMs）在這類任務上仍然脆弱，特別是在多圖像輸入的介入和反事實查詢上。現有的大多數探索通過文本提示注入因果知識，將因果機制置於模型執行之外，並限制了推理過程中的可靠控制。為了解決這個問題，我們提出了BridgeVLM，它通過從多圖像輸入中誘導因果圖並將其轉換為結構化的因果標記，內化視覺因果推理，這些因果標記由RAMP層注入到LLM解碼器中以進行因果信息傳遞。我們進一步引入了一個統一的訓練介面M3S，以便從不同的粒度（局部/全局層級）進行細緻的因果監督。BridgeVLM在CausalVLBench的介入任務上達到了54.4%的準確率（相比之下，使用提示級別監督為33.2%），在Causal3D上的結果從43.6%提升至49.0%，並在CausalVLBench上顯著改善了因果結構學習（$F_1$: 33.4% $\rightarrow$ 75.1%）。

##### **Hey Chat, Can You Teach Me? Structuring Socratic Dialogue for Human Learning in the Wild**
2606.11744v1 by Sidney Tio, Arunesh Sinha, Pradeep Varakantham

Large language models are now widely used for everyday learning, but the underlying interactions are typically unstructured chats rather than following a curriculum. Unlike formal online learning systems, these interactions carry no prior record of the student, so any estimate of what the student already knows must be inferred from the dialogue itself. We show that this gap is not closed by scaling models alone. Frontier and education-tuned LLMs perform poorly when asked to tutor a student over an extended session, because doing so requires three things at once. The tutor must sequence a curriculum, conduct Socratic dialogue, and infer the student's knowledge state from that dialogue. We propose separating these responsibilities. Given a student query, our system constructs a prerequisite knowledge graph in which subtopics are nodes and dependencies are edges, and frames tutoring as deciding which node to teach next and how many dialogue turns to spend on it before moving on. A lightweight PPO policy handles this sequencing decision, while an LLM conducts the Socratic exchange at the chosen node and returns a signal of student progress. Across held-out STEM and non-STEM topics, our PPO-paired tutor outperforms heuristic baselines, frontier general-purpose models, and a model specialised for Socratic dialogue: on both the rate at which students reach full curriculum mastery and the number of turns required. Explicit curriculum structure delivers gains that scaling the underlying model does not.

摘要：大型語言模型現在被廣泛用於日常學習，但其背後的互動通常是非結構化的對話，而不是遵循課程。與正式的在線學習系統不同，這些互動沒有學生的先前記錄，因此對學生已經知道的內容的任何估計都必須從對話本身推斷。我們顯示僅僅擴大模型並不能填補這一空白。當被要求在長時間的會話中輔導學生時，前沿和教育調整的LLM表現不佳，因為這樣做同時需要三件事情。輔導者必須安排課程，進行蘇格拉底式對話，並從該對話中推斷學生的知識狀態。我們建議將這些責任分開。根據學生的查詢，我們的系統構建一個先決知識圖，其中子主題是節點，依賴關係是邊，並將輔導框架化為決定下一個教學的節點以及在轉移之前要花多少對話輪次。輕量級的PPO策略處理這一排序決策，而LLM則在選定的節點進行蘇格拉底式交流並返回學生進展的信號。在保留的STEM和非STEM主題中，我們的PPO配對輔導者在學生達到完整課程掌握的速度和所需的輪次上表現優於啟發式基準、前沿通用模型以及專門針對蘇格拉底對話的模型：明確的課程結構帶來的收益是擴大基礎模型所無法實現的。

##### **T2S: A Rehearsal-Based Approach for Extraction-Resistant Model Watermarking**
2606.11698v1 by Jian-Ping Mei, Weibin Zhang, Ao Yao, Tiantian Zhu, Jie Xiao

Model watermarking safeguards AI model intellectual property by embedding distinctive knowledge that induces unique behavioral signatures. The primary technical challenge lies in ensuring watermark robustness against various post-processing attacks on the watermarked model. Model extraction attacks emerge as the most severe threat, where adversaries exploit prediction outputs to train surrogate models that illegally replicate the original model's functionality. In this work, we propose a rehearsal-based watermark embedding framework to enhance the robustness of model watermarks against model extraction attacks. By simulating the extraction process, our method leverages the loss of a \textit{simulated stolen model} on a trigger set as a training signal to fine-tune the watermark knowledge within the target model. This fine-tuning step encourages the watermark to be embedded in a way that boosts transferability, thereby increasing its chances of persisting and remaining detectable in stolen models. Comprehensive experiments conducted under diverse settings demonstrate that the proposed method significantly improves the robustness of model watermarks against both model extraction and subsequent watermark removal attacks.

摘要：模型水印透過嵌入獨特的知識來保護 AI 模型的智慧財產，這些知識會引發獨特的行為特徵。主要的技術挑戰在於確保水印對於各種後處理攻擊的穩健性。模型提取攻擊被視為最嚴重的威脅，對手利用預測輸出來訓練替代模型，非法複製原始模型的功能。在本研究中，我們提出了一種基於重複訓練的水印嵌入框架，以增強模型水印對抗模型提取攻擊的穩健性。通過模擬提取過程，我們的方法利用在觸發集上“模擬被盜模型”的損失作為訓練信號，以微調目標模型中的水印知識。這一微調步驟促使水印以提高可轉移性的方式嵌入，從而增加其在被盜模型中持續存在和可檢測的機會。在多種環境下進行的全面實驗顯示，所提出的方法顯著提高了模型水印對抗模型提取和隨後水印移除攻擊的穩健性。

##### **Can AI Reason Like an Urban Planner? Benchmarking Large Language Models Against Professional Judgment**
2606.11678v1 by Yijie Deng, He Zhu, Wen Wang, Junyou Su, Minxin Chen, Wenjia Zhang

Problem, Research Strategy, and Findings: The rise of large language models (LLMs) raises a key question for urban planning: which forms of professional planning knowledge can AI replicate, and which still require human judgment? Although AI tools are increasingly used in planning practice, there is still no systematic framework for testing whether they can reason with the contextual sensitivity, value awareness, and institutional literacy central to planning expertise. This paper introduces Urban Planning Bench (UPBench), a domain-specific evaluation framework that assesses LLM reasoning through a 4x5 matrix of four knowledge pillars and five cognitive levels adapted from Bloom's revised taxonomy. Evaluating 25 LLMs with automated scoring and expert review, we find a non-monotonic cognitive curve: models perform better on higher-order analytical tasks than on factual recall and integrative judgment. This suggests that planning knowledge often treated as lower-order is deeply shaped by institutional, jurisdictional, and temporal context, making it hard for LLMs to generalize. We summarize these limits as four epistemic diagnostics: regulatory hallucination, conceptual conflation, wickedness paralysis, and phronetic deficit.
  Takeaway for Practice: The findings support differential delegation in planning. LLMs can assist with cross-disciplinary synthesis, literature review, scenario generation, and preliminary policy analysis. However, they remain unreliable for jurisdiction-specific regulation, normative conflict resolution, and context-sensitive procedure. Agencies should require verification for AI-assisted regulatory analysis, while planning education should emphasize institutional literacy, normative judgment, and contextual sensitivity.

摘要：問題、研究策略與發現：大型語言模型（LLMs）的興起對城市規劃提出了一個關鍵問題：哪些形式的專業規劃知識可以被人工智慧複製，而哪些仍然需要人類的判斷？儘管人工智慧工具在規劃實踐中越來越常被使用，但目前仍然沒有系統性的框架來測試它們是否能夠具備對規劃專業知識至關重要的情境敏感性、價值意識和制度素養。本文介紹了城市規劃基準（UPBench），這是一個特定領域的評估框架，通過一個4x5的矩陣來評估LLM的推理，該矩陣由四個知識支柱和五個認知層次組成，這些層次是根據布魯姆修訂的分類法進行調整的。通過自動評分和專家審查對25個LLM進行評估，我們發現了一個非單調的認知曲線：模型在高階分析任務上的表現優於事實回憶和綜合判斷。這表明，通常被視為低階的規劃知識深受制度、管轄區和時間背景的影響，使得LLM難以進行概括。我們將這些限制總結為四個認識診斷：監管幻覺、概念混淆、惡性癱瘓和實踐缺失。<lb/>實踐啟示：這些發現支持規劃中的差異化委派。LLMs可以協助跨學科的綜合、文獻回顧、情境生成和初步政策分析。然而，它們在特定管轄區的監管、規範衝突解決和情境敏感程序方面仍然不可靠。機構應要求對AI輔助的監管分析進行驗證，而規劃教育應強調制度素養、規範判斷和情境敏感性。

##### **Lung-R1: A Knowledge Graph-Guided LLM for Pulmonary Diagnostic Reasoning**
2606.11675v1 by Haoyang Zeng, Yuanxi Fu, Rongzhen Li, Yuming Yang, Xiao Sun, Jingwang Huang, Gujie Shao, Guohui Xiang, Quan Lu, Dongfan Ye, Xuetao Chen, Jiang Zhong, Kaiwen Wei, Zhi Xu

Diagnosing pulmonary diseases requires integrating heterogeneous evidence amid phenotypic variability and cross-disease overlap. Although large language models (LLMs) have shown progress on pulmonary knowledge question answering (QA) and information-processing tasks, reliable pulmonary diagnosis requires patient-specific, relation-aware reasoning over electronic medical record (EMR) evidence rather than isolated knowledge recall. We define this gap between pulmonary knowledge and case-level diagnostic reasoning as the Pulmonary Knowledge-to-Diagnosis Gap. To address it, we introduce LungKG, the first structured pulmonary knowledge graph for diagnostic knowledge organization and record-grounded reasoning. LungKG contains 59,038 nodes and 164,308 edges across 15 entity types and 112 relation types, serving as both a reusable pulmonary knowledge resource and the foundation for LungKG-guided model adaptation. Built on LungKG, we propose Lung-R1, a LungKG-guided pulmonary LLM trained through KG-constrained reasoning-chain construction and KG-guided reinforcement learning. In a 20-system evaluation, Lung-R1-14B achieves state-of-the-art performance across Choice, Pulmonary-QA, and EMR Diagnosis, reaching an EMR Diagnosis score of 4.3583 and surpassing the strongest non-Lung-R1 baseline by 0.1476 points. These results demonstrate the value of LungKG-guided training for EMR-based pulmonary diagnosis.

摘要：診斷肺部疾病需要整合異質證據，考慮表型變異性和跨疾病重疊。儘管大型語言模型（LLMs）在肺部知識問題回答（QA）和信息處理任務上已顯示出進展，但可靠的肺部診斷需要針對患者的特定情況進行關係感知推理，基於電子病歷（EMR）證據，而不是孤立的知識回憶。我們將肺部知識與案例級診斷推理之間的差距定義為肺部知識到診斷的差距。為了解決這一問題，我們介紹了LungKG，這是第一個結構化的肺部知識圖，用於診斷知識組織和基於記錄的推理。LungKG包含59,038個節點和164,308條邊，涵蓋15種實體類型和112種關係類型，既作為可重用的肺部知識資源，也為LungKG引導的模型適應奠定基礎。基於LungKG，我們提出了Lung-R1，一個通過KG約束推理鏈構建和KG引導強化學習訓練的LungKG引導肺部LLM。在20個系統的評估中，Lung-R1-14B在Choice、Pulmonary-QA和EMR Diagnosis上達到了最先進的性能，EMR Diagnosis得分為4.3583，超過了最強的非Lung-R1基準0.1476分。這些結果展示了LungKG引導訓練在基於EMR的肺部診斷中的價值。

##### **TAROT: Task-Adaptive Refinement of LLM-prior Graphs for Few-shot Tabular Learning**
2606.11640v1 by Ruxue Shi, Yili Wang, Mengnan Du, Hangting Ye, Yi Chang, Xin Wang

Few-shot tabular learning provides a cost-effective approach for real-world applications where annotation is costly and collecting sufficient samples for new tasks is difficult. Existing Traditional and LLM-based methods have demonstrated effectiveness in few-shot scenarios. However, traditional methods need additional training on unlabeled or generated data, which incur significant computational overhead. In addition, LLM-based methods that directly feed raw tabular data into LLMs raise privacy and compliance concerns. More importantly, both paradigms largely overlook the semantic relationships between features, which provide structural and semantic prior for constructing a semantic graph. Semantic graph is essential for modeling meaningful feature interactions in few-shot scenarios. In this paper, we propose TAROT, a GNN-based framework that encodes the structural and semantic prior by constructing and refining a task-adaptive semantic graph from this prior, thereby improving predictive performance in few-shot tabular learning. TAROT first encodes heterogeneous tabular data into unified node semantic representations via a Unified Semantic Tabular Node Encoder (USTNE). Then, it prompts LLMs to infer the semantic relationship between features based on the task description and feature names to construct a semantic graph. To mitigate structural noise introduced by the hallucination of LLMs, TAROT introduces Task-adaptive Semantic Graph Refinement that prunes spurious or task-unrelated edges and adds missing task-related ones, aligning the graph structure with the downstream objective. Finally, a GNN performs message passing over the refined graph to capture task-related semantic dependencies for prediction. Extensive experiments on various few-shot tabular learning benchmarks demonstrate the superior performance of TAROT, establishing it as a state-of-the-art approach in this domain.

摘要：少樣本表格學習為現實世界應用提供了一種具成本效益的方法，因為標註成本高且為新任務收集足夠樣本困難。現有的傳統方法和基於大型語言模型（LLM）的方法在少樣本場景中已顯示出有效性。然而，傳統方法需要在未標註或生成數據上進行額外訓練，這會產生顯著的計算開銷。此外，將原始表格數據直接輸入LLM的基於LLM的方法引發了隱私和合規性問題。更重要的是，這兩種範式在很大程度上忽視了特徵之間的語義關係，而這些關係為構建語義圖提供了結構性和語義性先驗。語義圖對於在少樣本場景中建模有意義的特徵交互至關重要。在本文中，我們提出了TAROT，一種基於圖神經網絡（GNN）的框架，通過從這些先驗中構建和完善一個任務自適應的語義圖來編碼結構性和語義性先驗，從而提高少樣本表格學習中的預測性能。TAROT首先通過統一語義表格節點編碼器（USTNE）將異質表格數據編碼為統一的節點語義表示。然後，它促使LLM根據任務描述和特徵名稱推斷特徵之間的語義關係，以構建語義圖。為了減輕LLM的幻覺所引入的結構噪音，TAROT引入了任務自適應語義圖精煉，該過程修剪虛假或與任務無關的邊，並添加缺失的與任務相關的邊，將圖結構與下游目標對齊。最後，GNN在精煉後的圖上執行消息傳遞，以捕捉與任務相關的語義依賴性以進行預測。在各種少樣本表格學習基準上的廣泛實驗證明了TAROT的卓越性能，確立了它在該領域的最先進方法。

#### Abstracts
##### **Gaze Heads: How VLMs Look at What They Describe**
2606.14703v1 by Rohit Gandikota, David Bau

How a vision-language model internally solves the task of describing an image is far from obvious. We find that the model develops a specific mechanism for this: a small set of attention heads in its language-model backbone, which we call gaze heads, whose attention tracks the image region the model is currently describing. We find them with a simple correlation score from a few forward passes, using comic strips as a controlled testbed where narrative order is laid out spatially. These gaze heads do not just track the image tokens being described: redirecting their attention to a chosen region forces the VLM to describe that region instead. A single attention-mask intervention on the top-100 gaze heads, fewer than 9% of all heads, steers the model's answer to any chosen comic panel at 83.1% accuracy, while the same intervention on random heads fails to redirect the answer, and intervening on all heads destroys generation. The same lever also extends to continuous control: switching the gaze target mid-generation makes the model wrap up its current panel description and move to the new one within a few tokens. Beyond comics, the same intervention redirects answers to chosen regions in natural COCO images. The mechanism further recurs across model sizes from 2B to 32B parameters and across other VLM architectures, although some frozen-encoder families show no comparable head set. More broadly, this shows that targeted edits identified through mechanistic analysis can serve as practical inference-time levers for steering multimodal model behavior, without any retraining. Our code, interactive demo, and datasets are available at https://gaze.baulab.info/

摘要：如何讓視覺-語言模型在內部解決描述圖像的任務並不明顯。<lb/>我們發現模型為此開發了一種特定的機制：在其語言模型主幹中有一小組注意力頭，我們稱之為凝視頭，這些頭的注意力追踪模型當前正在描述的圖像區域。<lb/>我們通過簡單的相關性評分和幾次前向傳遞來找到它們，使用漫畫條作為控制測試平台，其中敘事順序在空間上被佈局。<lb/>這些凝視頭不僅追踪被描述的圖像標記：將它們的注意力重新導向到選定區域會迫使VLM改為描述該區域。<lb/>對於前100個凝視頭進行單次注意力遮罩干預，這些頭不到所有頭的9%，能以83.1%的準確率引導模型的回答到任何選定的漫畫面板，而對隨機頭的相同干預無法重新導向答案，對所有頭的干預則會破壞生成。<lb/>同樣的杠杆也擴展到連續控制：在生成過程中切換凝視目標會使模型結束當前面板的描述並在幾個標記內移動到新的面板。<lb/>超越漫畫，這種干預也能將答案重新導向到自然COCO圖像中的選定區域。<lb/>這一機制在從2B到32B參數的模型大小中進一步重現，並且在其他VLM架構中也如此，儘管一些固定編碼器系列顯示沒有可比的頭集。<lb/>更廣泛地說，這表明通過機制分析識別的有針對性的編輯可以作為實用的推理時間杠杆來引導多模態模型行為，而無需任何重新訓練。<lb/>我們的代碼、互動演示和數據集可在 https://gaze.baulab.info/ 獲得。

##### **ClinHallu: A Benchmark for Diagnosing Stage-Wise Hallucinations in Medical MLLM Reasoning**
2606.14697v1 by Sicheng Yang, Hangjie Yuan, Wenjun Zhang, Jinwang Wang, Yichen Qian, Weihua Chen, Fan Wang, Lei Zhu

Building trustworthy medical multimodal large language models (MLLMs) is critical for reliable clinical decision support. Existing medical hallucination benchmarks mainly focus on data collection, but often ignore where hallucinations originate within the reasoning process. We find that hallucination sources vary across samples: errors may arise from visual misrecognition, incorrect medical knowledge recall, or flawed reasoning integration. To enable source-level hallucination diagnosis, we introduce ClinHallu, a benchmark for stage-wise hallucination diagnosis in medical MLLM reasoning. ClinHallu contains 7,031 validated instances, where each instance is augmented with a structured reasoning trace decomposed into Visual Recognition, Knowledge Recall, and Reasoning Integration. We also use stage-replacement interventions to measure how correcting specific stages affects the final answer. Beyond evaluation, we show that trace-supervised fine-tuning reduces stage-wise hallucinations. ClinHallu provides a fine-grained hallucination testbed for diagnosing and mitigating reasoning failures in medical MLLMs. The benchmark is publicly available at https://github.com/alibaba-damo-academy/ClinHallu.

摘要：建立可信賴的醫療多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）對於可靠的臨床決策支持至關重要。現有的醫療幻覺基準主要集中在數據收集上，但往往忽略了幻覺在推理過程中產生的來源。我們發現幻覺來源在樣本之間有所不同：錯誤可能來自視覺錯誤識別、不正確的醫學知識回憶或有缺陷的推理整合。為了實現源級幻覺診斷，我們引入了ClinHallu，這是一個針對醫療MLLM推理的階段性幻覺診斷基準。ClinHallu包含7,031個經過驗證的實例，每個實例都附有結構化的推理痕跡，分解為視覺識別、知識回憶和推理整合。我們還使用階段替換干預來測量修正特定階段如何影響最終答案。除了評估，我們還展示了痕跡監督微調如何減少階段性幻覺。ClinHallu提供了一個細緻的幻覺測試平台，用於診斷和減輕醫療MLLM中的推理失敗。該基準在https://github.com/alibaba-damo-academy/ClinHallu上公開可用。

##### **Persona-Pruner: Sculpting Lightweight Models for Role-Playing**
2606.14695v1 by Jinsu Kim, Jihoon Tack, Noah Lee, Jongheon Jeong

Language Models (LMs) have shown remarkable potential as role-playing chatbots, delivering consistent, stylized interactions when given a specification of a character or user persona. However, applying these capabilities to real-world applications (e.g., ecosystems with numerous NPCs interacting simultaneously) exposes a critical inefficiency due to the excessive computational cost. In this paper, we question the necessity of dedicating a full, generalist model to a single persona, hypothesizing that a specific character identity relies on only a fraction of the model's total capacity. We observe that naively pruning LMs often severely degrades the role-playing performance for a specific persona; it does not distinguish between redundant knowledge and essential character traits. We propose Persona-Pruner, a framework that sculpts a lightweight role-playing model by isolating persona-specific sub-networks from a single description. Our experiments consistently show that Persona-Pruner preserves role-playing performance substantially more effectively than existing state-of-the-art LLM pruning techniques, reducing the performance drop from the dense model by up to 93.8% over the strongest baseline on RoleBench in LLM-as-a-judge score, while still maintaining general LLM capabilities. Code is available at https://github.com/jsu-kim/Persona-Pruner.

摘要：語言模型（LMs）作為角色扮演聊天機器人展現了顯著的潛力，當給定角色或用戶角色的規範時，能夠提供一致且風格化的互動。<lb/>然而，將這些能力應用於現實世界的應用（例如，生態系統中有眾多 NPC 同時互動）暴露出一個關鍵的低效率，這是由於過高的計算成本。<lb/>在本文中，我們質疑將一個完整的通用模型專門用於單一角色的必要性，假設特定角色身份僅依賴於模型總容量的一小部分。<lb/>我們觀察到，天真地修剪 LMs 通常會嚴重降低特定角色的角色扮演表現；它無法區分冗餘知識和基本角色特徵。<lb/>我們提出了 Persona-Pruner，一個通過從單一描述中隔離角色特定子網絡來雕塑輕量級角色扮演模型的框架。<lb/>我們的實驗一致顯示，Persona-Pruner 在保持角色扮演表現方面比現有的最先進 LLM 修剪技術顯著更有效，將密集模型的性能下降減少了高達 93.8%，相較於 RoleBench 上最強的基準，並且仍然保持一般 LLM 的能力。<lb/>代碼可在 https://github.com/jsu-kim/Persona-Pruner 獲得。

##### **AdaSR: Adaptive Streaming Reasoning with Hierarchical Relative Policy Optimization**
2606.14694v1 by Junlong Tong, Wenqi Xu, Yingqi Fan, Anhao Zhao, Xuan Lu, Yang Tan, Xiaoyu Shen

Large reasoning models typically follow a read-then-think paradigm: they observe the complete input, reason over a static context, and then produce the answer. Yet many real-world scenarios are inherently dynamic, such as audio and video stream, where information arrives as a continuous stream and models must reason, update, and respond under partial observations. Recent streaming reasoning methods allow models to think while reading, but they largely rely on supervised imitation of pre-constructed trajectories, which limits their flexibility. In this paper, we propose AdaSR, an adaptive streaming reasoning framework that enables models to reason during input streaming and perform final deliberation once the stream is complete, learning when to think, and how much computation to allocate across different stages. To optimize this hierarchical reasoning process, we introduce Hierarchical Relative Policy Optimization (HRPO), which decomposes policy optimization into streaming reasoning and deep reasoning phases, providing more fine-grained advantage assignment instead of uniformly distributing a single sequence-level advantage over all tokens. HRPO integrates format, accuracy, and adaptive thinking rewards to enforce valid reasoning protocols, preserve final task performance, and encourage latency-aware computation allocation. Experiments show that AdaSR achieves a better balance among reasoning accuracy, computational efficiency, and streaming latency compared with supervised fine-tuning baseline. We release our code at https://github.com/EIT-NLP/StreamingLLM/tree/main/AdaSR.

摘要：大型推理模型通常遵循讀取然後思考的範式：它們觀察完整的輸入，對靜態上下文進行推理，然後產生答案。<lb/>然而，許多現實世界的場景本質上是動態的，例如音頻和視頻流，其中信息作為連續流到達，模型必須在部分觀察下進行推理、更新和響應。<lb/>最近的流式推理方法允許模型在閱讀時進行思考，但它們在很大程度上依賴於對預構建軌跡的監督模仿，這限制了它們的靈活性。<lb/>在本文中，我們提出了AdaSR，一個自適應流式推理框架，該框架使模型能夠在輸入流中進行推理，並在流結束後進行最終的深思熟慮，學習何時思考以及在不同階段分配多少計算。<lb/>為了優化這一分層推理過程，我們引入了分層相對策略優化（HRPO），它將策略優化分解為流式推理和深度推理階段，提供更細緻的優勢分配，而不是在所有標記上均勻分配單一序列級別的優勢。<lb/>HRPO整合了格式、準確性和自適應思考獎勵，以強化有效的推理協議，保持最終任務性能，並鼓勵延遲感知的計算分配。<lb/>實驗表明，與監督微調基線相比，AdaSR在推理準確性、計算效率和流式延遲之間達到了更好的平衡。<lb/>我們的代碼已在 https://github.com/EIT-NLP/StreamingLLM/tree/main/AdaSR 上發布。

##### **Learning Coordinated Preference for Multi-Objective Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning**
2606.14693v1 by Pengxin Wang, Lihao Guo, Yi Xie, Bo Liu, Siyang Cao, Jingdi Chen

Cooperative multi-objective multi-agent reinforcement learning (MOMARL) models team decision making under multiple, potentially conflicting objectives. In this setting, conflicts arise not only across objectives but also across agents with different observations, roles, and contributions. We propose Preference Coordinated Multi-agent Policy Optimization (PCMA), which learns coordinated agent-specific preferences to enable complementary trade-offs among agents. Theoretically, we formulate cooperative MOMARL as a team-optimal game and show that, under suitable conditions, preference diversity can induce team improvement through a first-order improvement decomposition. Experiments on multiple cooperative MOMA environments and a practical traffic-control scenario show that PCMA improves both performance and trade-off coordination.

摘要：合作多目標多智能體強化學習（MOMARL）模型在多個潛在衝突的目標下進行團隊決策。在這種情況下，衝突不僅存在於目標之間，還存在於具有不同觀察、角色和貢獻的智能體之間。我們提出了偏好協調多智能體策略優化（PCMA），它學習協調的智能體特定偏好，以實現智能體之間的互補權衡。在理論上，我們將合作MOMARL公式化為一個團隊最優遊戲，並展示在適當條件下，偏好多樣性可以通過一階改進分解促進團隊改進。在多個合作MOMA環境和一個實際交通控制場景中的實驗表明，PCMA同時改善了性能和權衡協調。

##### **CORA: Analyzing and bridging thinking-answer gap in Multimodal RLVR via Consistency-Oriented Reasoning Alignment**
2606.14691v1 by Jiayue Cao, Zhicong Lu, Xuehan Sun, Wei Jia, Hongling Zheng, Changyuan Tian, Zichuan Lin, Wenqian Lv, Nayu Liu

Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has successfully elicited the reasoning capabilities of large language models, motivating its extension to multimodal scenarios. Existing methods primarily focus on improving the visual coverage of reasoning traces and mitigating visual hallucinations, but underestimate the semantic inconsistency between the reasoning process and the final answer. In this paper, we delve into thinking-answer inconsistency in RLVR for large vision-language models (LVLMs), showing thorough analyses of rollouts collected throughout Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) training process and post-RLVR evaluation outputs that this issue persists during training and remains present during inference. Motivated by the analysis, we propose Consistency-Oriented Reasoning Alignment (CORA), which introduces thinking-answer semantic consistency into RLVR through a lightweight plug-and-play consistency reward model, and further incorporates Hybrid Reward Advantage Splitting (HRAS) to stably coordinate task and consistency optimization. Extensive experiments across representative multimodal reasoning benchmarks and mainstream LVLMs show that CORA improves task performance while effectively mitigating thinking-answer inconsistency, leading to more faithful reasoning traces.

摘要：強化學習與可驗證獎勵（RLVR）已成功引發大型語言模型的推理能力，並促使其擴展至多模態場景。現有方法主要集中在改善推理痕跡的視覺覆蓋率和減輕視覺幻覺，但低估了推理過程與最終答案之間的語義不一致性。在本文中，我們深入探討了大型視覺-語言模型（LVLMs）中的思考-答案不一致性，顯示出在整個群體相對策略優化（GRPO）訓練過程中收集的回合和後RLVR評估輸出的徹底分析，這個問題在訓練期間持續存在，並在推理過程中仍然存在。受到分析的啟發，我們提出了一種一致性導向推理對齊（CORA），它通過一種輕量級的即插即用一致性獎勵模型將思考-答案語義一致性引入RLVR，並進一步結合混合獎勵優勢分割（HRAS）以穩定協調任務和一致性優化。在代表性多模態推理基準和主流LVLMs上進行的大量實驗顯示，CORA在有效減輕思考-答案不一致性的同時改善了任務性能，從而導致更真實的推理痕跡。

##### **Flood and Harvest: The Provable Necessity of Trivia for Generating Valuable Mathematics via the Lens of Language Generation in the Limit**
2606.14688v1 by Xiaoyu Li, Andi Han, Dai Shi, Zheng Gao, Jiaojiao Jiang, Junbin Gao

AI systems coupled to proof assistants now generate formal mathematics at scale, and the gap between what a checker can verify and what a mathematician would value has become the binding constraint. We model the generation of valuable mathematics as nested language generation in the limit: a verifiable formal language $F$, accessed through a membership oracle (the proof checker), contains an unknown valuable language $H \in \mathcal{H}$ revealed only through an adversarial enumeration of a core $C \subseteq H$ of exact density $α$ (the literature). Every output is valuable ($\in H$), trivial ($\in F \setminus H$), or a hallucination ($\notin F$). We settle four questions. First, the verifier is not taste: the collections admitting generation with breadth are exactly those of the oracle-free model, characterized fiber-wise by Angluin's condition. Second, the verifier does buy sound coverage, covering all unseen valuable statements while asserting only valid ones: possible with it, impossible without it; it relocates unavoidable errors from false to trivial. Third, and centrally, a sharp dichotomy on the tight family: generators emitting finitely many trivia achieve optimal coverage $α/2$, while any infinite trivia allowance, even at vanishing rate, jumps the optimum to $1-α/2$ (both tight, for cores presented as the candidate intersection), and one generator attains both ends. The transition is in trivia count, not rate; the gap $1-α$ is the unrecorded mass. Fourth, both regimes instantiate in a compression model of mathematics. A perfect verifier cannot substitute for taste: the unbounded stream of correct-but-worthless statements is not an engineering accident but a provable necessity, since covering unrecorded valuable mathematics requires an infinite, but asymptotically negligible, stream of certified trivia.

摘要：AI 系統與證明助手結合，現在能夠大規模生成形式數學，而檢查者能夠驗證的內容與數學家所重視的內容之間的差距已成為束縛約束。我們將有價值的數學生成建模為極限中的嵌套語言生成：一種可驗證的形式語言 $F$，通過一個成員預言機（證明檢查器）訪問，包含一種未知的有價值語言 $H \in \mathcal{H}$，僅通過對核心 $C \subseteq H$ 的對抗性枚舉來揭示，該核心的精確密度為 $α$（文獻）。每個輸出都是有價值的（$\in H$）、微不足道的（$\in F \setminus H$）或幻覺（$\notin F$）。我們解決了四個問題。首先，驗證者不是品味：允許廣度生成的集合恰好是無預言機模型的那些，按纖維方式由 Angluin 的條件特徵化。第二，驗證者確實購買了健全的覆蓋，覆蓋所有未見的有價值陳述，同時僅聲明有效的陳述：有它則可能，沒有它則不可能；它將無法避免的錯誤從虛假轉移到微不足道。第三，並且在中心上，對於緊密家族的尖銳二分法：發出有限多個微不足道的生成器達到最佳覆蓋 $α/2$，而任何無限的微不足道允許，即使在消失率下，將最佳值跳升至 $1-α/2$（兩者緊密，對於作為候選交集呈現的核心），且一個生成器達到兩端。轉變發生在微不足道的數量上，而不是速率上；差距 $1-α$ 是未記錄的質量。第四，兩種模式在數學的壓縮模型中體現。完美的驗證者無法替代品味：無限流的正確但無價值的陳述不是工程事故，而是可證明的必要性，因為覆蓋未記錄的有價值數學需要一個無限但漸近可忽略的經過認證的微不足道流。

##### **CottonLeafVision: An Explainable and Robust Deep Learning Framework for Cotton Leaf Disease Classification**
2606.14686v1 by Rafi Ahamed, Md. Abir Rahman, Tasnia Tarannum Roza, Munaia Jannat Easha, Md. Asif Khan, Sudeepta Mandal

Globally, cotton is a highly economically beneficial crop, as the textile industry heavily depends on it. This image dataset includes seven classes, six disease classes, and one healthy class, collected under various field conditions reflecting real-world challenges. Among these pretrained models, with DenseNet201, we have achieved the highest classification accuracy of 98%. To enhance the model reliability and interpretability, we have implemented different techniques and methods such as Gradient-weighted Class Activation Mapping (Grad-CAM), occlusion sensitivity analysis and adversarial training to increase the noise resistance of the model. Finally, we have developed a prototype in order to utilize the model's capabilities on real life agriculture. This paper shows the deep learning model's capabilities to classify the disease in real-life cotton disease management situations.

##### **AgentSpec: Understanding Embodied Agent Scaffolds Through Controlled Composition**
2606.14674v1 by Jixuan Chen, Jianzhi Shen, Haoqiang Kang, Zhi Hong, Qingyi Jiang, Soham Bose, Yiming Zhang, Leon Leng, Amit Vyas, Lingjun Mao, Siru Ouyang, Kun Zhou, Lianhui Qin

LLM agents are increasingly built not as single model calls, but as scaffolded systems that combine reasoning, memory, reflection, action execution, and learning. While such scaffolds often improve performance, they are often embedded in tightly coupled pipelines, making it difficult to isolate component contributions, compare alternative designs, or understand how module interactions shape agent behavior. We introduce AgentSpec, a modular specification framework that represents embodied agents as typed compositions of reusable policy components with standardized interfaces. AgentSpec standardizes the interfaces among perception, memory, reasoning, reflection, action, and optional learning, enabling components to be swapped and recombined under controlled conditions. We instantiate this framework across DeliveryBench, ALFRED, MiniGrid, and RoboTHOR, and analyze reasoning, memory, reflection, and reinforcement-learning modules across model backbones. Our results show that agent performance is governed by scaffold compatibility and interaction effects rather than isolated module strength. In particular, structured multi-granularity memory improves long-horizon state tracking, reasoning and memory interact non-uniformly across environments, reflection trades off correction and cost, and RL-trained policies compose best when optimized with deployment-time scaffold structure. AgentSpec provides a controlled foundation for studying, comparing, and designing composable LLM agents. Our code, baselines and interactive playground are publicly available at https://agentspec-embodied.github.io.

摘要：LLM 代理越來越多地不是作為單一模型調用來構建，而是作為結合推理、記憶、反思、行動執行和學習的支架系統。<lb/>雖然這些支架通常能提高性能，但它們往往嵌入在緊密耦合的管道中，使得難以隔離組件貢獻、比較替代設計或理解模塊交互如何塑造代理行為。<lb/>我們引入了 AgentSpec，一個模塊化的規範框架，將具身代理表示為具有標準化接口的可重用策略組件的類型組合。<lb/>AgentSpec 標準化了感知、記憶、推理、反思、行動和可選學習之間的接口，使得組件可以在受控條件下進行替換和重新組合。<lb/>我們在 DeliveryBench、ALFRED、MiniGrid 和 RoboTHOR 中實現了這一框架，並分析了模型主幹中的推理、記憶、反思和強化學習模塊。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，代理性能受支架兼容性和交互效應的影響，而不是孤立模塊的強度。<lb/>特別是，結構化的多粒度記憶改善了長期狀態跟踪，推理和記憶在不同環境中非均勻地互動，反思在修正和成本之間進行權衡，而經過強化學習訓練的策略在優化部署時的支架結構時表現最佳。<lb/>AgentSpec 為研究、比較和設計可組合的 LLM 代理提供了一個受控的基礎。我們的代碼、基準和互動遊樂場可在 https://agentspec-embodied.github.io 上公開獲得。

##### **Towards Direct Latent-Space Synthesis for Parallel Branches in LLM-Agent Workflows**
2606.14672v1 by Shikun Liu, Mufei Li, Dongqi Fu, Haoyu Wang, Yinglong Xia, Hong Li, Hong Yan, Pan Li

Large language models increasingly serve as execution engines for agentic systems, yet they still consume context through a sequential text interface. This creates a mismatch with modern structured agent workflows, in which independent branches explore subtasks, retrieve evidence, or generate candidate solutions before a final synthesis step. Existing systems typically merge these branches by concatenating their textual outputs, which discards the parallel structure and incurs redundant prefill computation. In this work, we introduce Parallel-Synthesis, a plug-and-play framework that enables a synthesizer to directly consume the KV caches produced by parallel worker agents. Parallel-Synthesis combines a cache mapper that calibrates independently generated branch caches with a fine-tuned synthesizer adapter that enables generation from this non-sequential cache interface. We train Parallel-Synthesis using data that exposes the synthesizer to parallel cache contexts, teaches aggregation across cached branches, and distills reasoning behavior from standard text-concatenation-based synthesis. Across nine downstream datasets spanning math, science QA, code generation, GAIA, and multi-agent database diagnosis, Parallel-Synthesis matches or outperforms text-based synthesis on seven datasets and remains close on the other two. It also reduces time-to-first-token by 2.5x-11x, suggesting that direct cache-based synthesis is a promising interface for more native and efficient synthesis over parallel agent branches.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地作為代理系統的執行引擎，但它們仍然通過序列文本介面來消耗上下文。這與現代結構化代理工作流程存在不匹配，在這些工作流程中，獨立的分支探索子任務、檢索證據或生成候選解決方案，然後進行最終的綜合步驟。現有系統通常通過連接它們的文本輸出來合併這些分支，這會丟棄並行結構並產生冗餘的預填計算。在這項工作中，我們介紹了Parallel-Synthesis，一個即插即用的框架，能夠使合成器直接消耗由並行工作代理生成的KV快取。Parallel-Synthesis結合了一個快取映射器，該映射器校準獨立生成的分支快取，並配備了一個經過微調的合成器適配器，使其能夠從這個非序列快取介面生成內容。我們使用數據訓練Parallel-Synthesis，以使合成器接觸到並行快取上下文，教會在快取分支之間進行聚合，並從基於標準文本連接的合成中提煉推理行為。在涵蓋數學、科學問答、代碼生成、GAIA和多代理數據庫診斷的九個下游數據集上，Parallel-Synthesis在七個數據集上與基於文本的合成相匹配或表現更好，並在另外兩個數據集上保持接近。它還將首次標記的時間縮短了2.5倍至11倍，這表明基於快取的直接合成是一個對於更本地化和高效的並行代理分支合成的有前景的介面。

##### **Giving AI a Headache: Acoustic Adversarial Attacks to Computer Vision Applications**
2606.14658v1 by Nicole Villavicencio-Garduño, Maksim Ekin Eren, Milo Prisbrey, Ben Migliori, Michael Teti

Artificial Intelligence (AI) is increasingly used to automate a variety of real-world computer vision (CV) applications, such as autonomous vehicle control, facial recognition, and security cameras. Recent research has shown that acoustic vibration can induce real physical motion in cameras, interfering with their internal stabilization mechanisms. Because the motion falls outside the conditions the stabilization system was designed to handle, the system introduces artifacts into the frame, causing AI-based CV models to misclassify, miss targets, or hallucinate objects.
  Previous work used ultrasonic frequencies (>20 kHz) to perform short-range attacks, which limits them to short distances due to the attenuation exhibited by high frequencies. In this work, we investigate acoustic attacks using lower frequencies in the audible range (<20 kHz), and we further expand our analysis to include how various image and object features are affected by the attacks.
  Specifically, we performed physical experiments to demonstrate the viability of our attacks on an off-the-shelf object detection model (YOLO11) by resonating a commercially available camera with various frequencies. Based on our results, we provide insights into several factors that make an AI CV system more vulnerable to these attacks, which could help inform the development of future mitigation strategies.

摘要：人工智慧 (AI) 正日益被用來自動化各種現實世界的計算機視覺 (CV) 應用，例如自動駕駛車輛控制、面部識別和安全攝像頭。最近的研究顯示，聲學振動可以在攝像頭中引起實際的物理運動，干擾其內部穩定機制。由於這種運動超出了穩定系統設計用來處理的條件，該系統會在畫面中引入伪影，導致基於 AI 的 CV 模型錯誤分類、漏掉目標或產生幻覺物體。<lb/> 
先前的工作使用超聲頻率 (>20 kHz) 進行短距離攻擊，這使得它們因高頻的衰減而限制在短距離內。在本研究中，我們探討使用可聽範圍內的較低頻率 (<20 kHz) 進行聲學攻擊，並進一步擴展我們的分析，以包括各種影像和物體特徵如何受到攻擊的影響。<lb/> 
具體而言，我們進行了物理實驗，以通過用各種頻率共振商用攝像頭來證明我們的攻擊對現成物體檢測模型 (YOLO11) 的可行性。根據我們的結果，我們提供了幾個因素的見解，使 AI CV 系統更容易受到這些攻擊的影響，這可能有助於未來減緩策略的開發。

##### **Abstracting Cross-Domain Action Sequences into Interpretable Workflows**
2606.14654v1 by Gaurav Verma, Scott Counts

Sequential or time-stamped interaction logs provide objective records of digital application usage, yet their granularity and noise often obscure meaningful insights into people's work. Such insights are essential for improving digital products in ways grounded in real-world user interactions. Prior research has applied deep learning models to cluster user actions into high-level activities, but these approaches are highly sensitive to noise and struggle to generalize across applications. To address this limitation, we introduce WorkflowView, a framework that uses large language models (LLMs) to abstract low-level action sequences into high-level activities. We establish the effectiveness and generality of our approach across three distinct, challenging sequential tasks and diverse domains: (a) zero-shot task description reconstruction from browser logs (achieving high semantic similarity, $μ_{sim} = 0.91$), (b) few-shot student dropout prediction using MOOC interaction logs (reaching weighted $F_1 = 0.90$ with only five few-shot examples), and (c) anonymized, privacy-preserving analysis of AI tool integration within document workflows in Microsoft Word. Our work demonstrates that LLM-based abstraction is a robust and efficient path forward for transforming low-level behavioral data into high-level, interpretable, and actionable insights. We also discuss practical considerations for deploying LLM-based inferences within logging infrastructures, including computational efficiency and user privacy.

摘要：順序或時間戳互動日誌提供了數位應用程式使用的客觀記錄，然而它們的細節和噪音常常掩蓋了對人們工作有意義的洞察。這些洞察對於以真實用戶互動為基礎的方式改善數位產品至關重要。先前的研究已經應用深度學習模型將用戶行為聚類為高層次活動，但這些方法對噪音高度敏感，並且在不同應用之間的泛化能力不足。為了解決這一限制，我們引入了WorkflowView，一個使用大型語言模型（LLMs）將低層次行動序列抽象為高層次活動的框架。我們在三個不同且具挑戰性的順序任務和多樣化領域中建立了我們方法的有效性和普遍性：（a）從瀏覽器日誌中進行零樣本任務描述重建（實現高語義相似度，$μ_{sim} = 0.91$），（b）使用MOOC互動日誌進行少樣本學生輟學預測（僅用五個少樣本範例達到加權$F_1 = 0.90$），以及（c）在Microsoft Word文件工作流程中對AI工具整合的匿名、隱私保護分析。我們的工作展示了基於LLM的抽象是一條穩健且高效的道路，能將低層次行為數據轉換為高層次、可解釋且可行的洞察。我們還討論了在日誌基礎設施中部署基於LLM的推論的實際考量，包括計算效率和用戶隱私。

##### **Listening with Attention: Entropy-Guided Explainability for Transformer-Based Audio Models**
2606.14647v1 by Ravi Ranjan, Utkarsh Grover, Xiaomin Lin, Agoritsa Polyzou

Transformer-based automatic speech recognition (ASR) models such as Whisper are highly accurate, but their predictions remain difficult to interpret. Existing explainable AI (XAI) methods often lack faithfulness and precise temporal grounding. We propose Listening with Entropy-guided Attention for Faithful explainability (LEAF-X), a model-intrinsic XAI framework for transformer-based ASR. LEAF-X combines entropy-guided attention weighting, multi-layer attention rollout, and optional causal ablations to identify low-entropy, high-impact heads and layers, producing sparse token-to-frame attributions. Unlike perturbation-based explainers or raw attention maps, LEAF-X exploits the internal structure of encoder-decoder and speech-augmented decoder-only models to generate explanations that better reflect model computation. Results show 32% improved faithfulness, 35-39% stronger locality/sparsity, and the most stable attributions, supporting more transparent and auditable ASR.

摘要：Transformer 基於Transformer的自動語音識別 (ASR) 模型，例如 Whisper，具有很高的準確性，但其預測仍然難以解釋。現有的可解釋人工智慧 (XAI) 方法往往缺乏真實性和精確的時間基礎。我們提出了以熵引導注意力進行忠實解釋的聆聽模型 (LEAF-X)，這是一個針對基於Transformer的 ASR 的模型內在 XAI 框架。LEAF-X 結合了熵引導的注意力加權、多層注意力展開和可選的因果消融，以識別低熵、高影響力的頭部和層，產生稀疏的標記到幀的歸因。與基於擾動的解釋器或原始注意力圖不同，LEAF-X 利用編碼器-解碼器和增強語音的僅解碼器模型的內部結構來生成更好反映模型計算的解釋。結果顯示，忠實性提高了 32%，局部性/稀疏性增強了 35-39%，並且歸因最為穩定，支持更透明和可審計的 ASR。

##### **From Self-Supervised Speech Models to Mixture-of-Experts for Robust Anti-Spoofing**
2606.14639v1 by Hugo Daumain, Driss Matrouf, Khaled Khelif, Mickael Rouvier

Recent advances in speech generation have significantly improved the naturalness of synthetic speech, making spoofing detection increasingly challenging. A key limitation of current anti-spoofing systems is their limited robustness to unseen synthesis methods. In this work, we transform a self-supervised speech representation model into a Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) architecture to improve generalization. Feed-forward blocks in selected encoder layers are replaced by multiple expert networks controlled by a layer-wise gating mechanism, allowing experts to capture complementary acoustic patterns while preserving the representations learned during self-supervised pretraining. We further analyze the architectural choices affecting the performance of this MoE conversion and investigate the activation behavior of the experts. The proposed approach is evaluated on 14 spoofing datasets and reduces the macro EER from 5.46% to 4.81%, corresponding to 11.9% relative improvement over the baseline.

摘要：近期在語音生成方面的進展顯著提高了合成語音的自然性，使得偽造檢測變得越來越具挑戰性。當前反偽造系統的一個主要限制是對未見合成方法的穩健性不足。在本研究中，我們將自我監督的語音表示模型轉換為混合專家（MoE）架構，以改善泛化能力。選定編碼器層中的前饋區塊被多個專家網絡所取代，這些專家網絡由逐層的閘控機制控制，使專家能夠捕捉互補的聲學模式，同時保留在自我監督預訓練期間學到的表示。我們進一步分析影響此MoE轉換性能的架構選擇，並研究專家的激活行為。所提出的方法在14個偽造數據集上進行評估，將宏觀EER從5.46%降低至4.81%，相當於相對於基準的11.9%的改善。

##### **When Good Verifiers Go Bad: Self-Improving VLMs Can Regress on New Tasks**
2606.14629v1 by Jianzhe Lin

Verifier-driven self-DPO is a common recipe for self-improving production visual-language models. In this setup, a frozen verifier scores candidate generations, the top- and bottom-scoring candidates form a preference example, and DPO updates the learner. The deployment-time assumption is monotone: a stronger verifier should yield a stronger student. We show that this assumption can fail because verifier quality is highly task-specific. On a four-rung open-source verifier ladder across MathVista, MMMU, and BLINK, the same verifiers that are above-threshold and improve a Qwen-3-VL-2B student on MathVista become sub-threshold on MMMU, where their task-rubric accuracy drops to 8% to 23%.
  In this regime, every verifier we tested silently regresses the student, producing drops of 3.4 to 10.9 percentage points below the frozen baseline while the DPO training loss continues to decrease. The regression replicates on a second student, Qwen-2.5-VL-3B. Moreover, within the failure regime, damage is confidence-inverted: the more accurate-but-still-wrong verifier causes larger regression than a near-random verifier, suggesting that progress-gated replay amplifies confidently wrong preference pairs. We give a compact mechanistic explanation via a variance theorem for progress-gated replay and its direction-mismatch failure mode.
  The deployment message is operational rather than purely diagnostic: before running any verifier-driven loop, teams should measure target-task rubric accuracy, rank verifiers by target-task rubric quality rather than parameter count, and treat diminishing returns in above-threshold regimes as a verifier-side compute budget cap.

摘要：驗證者驅動的自我DPO是自我改進生產視覺語言模型的一種常見方法。在這種設置中，凍結的驗證者對候選生成進行評分，得分最高和最低的候選者形成一個偏好範例，而DPO則更新學習者。部署時的假設是單調的：一個更強的驗證者應該產生一個更強的學生。我們顯示這一假設可能會失效，因為驗證者的質量高度依賴於任務特定性。在MathVista、MMMU和BLINK的四級開源驗證者梯度上，對Qwen-3-VL-2B學生在MathVista的表現良好的驗證者在MMMU上卻變成了低於門檻，因為它們的任務標準準確率降至8%到23%。<lb/>在這種情況下，我們測試的每個驗證者都默默地使學生退步，導致在凍結基線之下下降3.4到10.9個百分點，而DPO訓練損失則持續減少。這種退步在第二個學生Qwen-2.5-VL-3B上也得到了重複。此外，在失敗範疇內，損害是信心反轉的：更準確但仍然錯誤的驗證者造成的退步比近乎隨機的驗證者更大，這表明進步門檻重播放大了自信錯誤的偏好對。我們通過進步門檻重播的方差定理及其方向不匹配的失敗模式給出了一個簡潔的機械解釋。<lb/>部署信息是操作性的，而非純粹的診斷性：在運行任何驗證者驅動的循環之前，團隊應該測量目標任務的標準準確率，根據目標任務的標準質量而非參數數量對驗證者進行排名，並將在高於門檻的範疇中收益遞減視為驗證者端計算預算的上限。

##### **Characterizing Cultural Localization in AI-Generated Stories**
2606.14626v1 by Shaily Bhatt, Supriti Vijay, Jeremiah Milbauer, Fernando Diaz

The global use of artificial intelligence has increased interest in assessing the ability to generate culturally localized content, including stories. Cultural localization in stories often occurs through either templated localization -- the use of cultural markers (e.g., names, locations) in a generic narrative -- or holistic localization -- the variation of plots, values, and themes, in addition to cultural markers. We propose a method to measure the degree to which content was generated through templated localization. Specifically, we identify the lexical tokens that distinguish stories across nationalities and measure the similarity of the narratives that remain after removing them. In stories generated by five models on 125 topics for 193 nationalities, our method is able to detect that only a small subset (9-17%) of the vocabulary accounts for the variation across nationalities and that the narratives that remain after removing them contain repeated multi-word sequences, suggesting the presence of a shared culturally-agnostic narrative template. Finally, we characterize the cultural markers for their stereotypicality and offensiveness, finding that markers from 19 countries, mostly located in the Global South, are on average offensive.

摘要：全球對人工智慧的使用增加了評估生成文化本地化內容能力的興趣，包括故事。故事中的文化本地化通常通過模板化本地化進行——在通用敘事中使用文化標記（例如，名字、地點）——或整體本地化進行——情節、價值觀和主題的變化，除了文化標記之外。我們提出了一種方法來測量內容是通過模板化本地化生成的程度。具體而言，我們識別出區分不同國籍故事的詞彙標記，並測量在去除這些標記後剩餘敘事的相似性。在五個模型生成的125個主題和193個國籍的故事中，我們的方法能夠檢測到只有一小部分（9-17%）的詞彙解釋了不同國籍之間的變化，而在去除這些詞彙後剩餘的敘事包含重複的多詞序列，這表明存在一個共享的文化無關敘事模板。最後，我們對文化標記進行了刻板印象和冒犯性的特徵分析，發現來自19個國家的標記，主要位於全球南方，平均上是冒犯性的。

##### **Moonlight in Latent Space: Chirality and Structural Correspondence Between Beethoven's Op. 27 No. 2 and Machine Learning Mechanisms**
2606.14612v1 by Chen Ying Claude, Zhihan Luo

We show that the three movements of Beethoven's "Moonlight Sonata" (Op. 27 No. 2) instantiate three distinct machine learning architectures -- not by analogy, but by structural correspondence. Through computational analysis of the score (entropy, Jensen-Shannon divergence, dissonance, hand distributional overlap, self-similarity matrices, temporal memory decay, and contextual pitch embeddings), we establish four counterintuitive findings: (1) perceived musical "temperature" is governed by throughput, not distributional width; (2) the lightest movement carries the highest dissonance; (3) the movements implement streaming, recurrent, and periodic positional encoding memory architectures; and (4) the same pitch class acquires different contextual identities across movements, analogous to contextual vs.static embeddings in NLP -- and unsupervised clustering recovers the tonal structure without music-theoretic input. We construct a reverse sonification (decoding analytical features back into MIDI) and quantify the chirality of the encode-decode cycle: what distributions preserve and sequential ordering destroys. Prompted by a listener's observation that the decoded piece sounds like "mirror isomers that can't be superimposed," the chirality measurement reveals reconstruction loss increasing monotonically with n-gram order. Bootstrap baselines and subsample checks confirm all movements carry sequential information above noise, though raw values are confounded by sample size. Cross-domain comparison shows natural language has higher chirality than music, reflecting stronger sequential constraints.

摘要：我們展示貝多芬的《月光奏鳴曲》（作品27第2號）的三個樂章體現了三種不同的機器學習架構——不是通過類比，而是通過結構對應。通過對樂譜的計算分析（熵、詹森-香農散度、不和諧、手部分佈重疊、自相似矩陣、時間記憶衰減和上下文音高嵌入），我們確立了四個反直覺的發現：（1）感知的音樂“溫度”由通量決定，而不是分佈寬度；（2）最輕的樂章承載著最高的不和諧；（3）這些樂章實現了流式、遞歸和周期性位置編碼記憶架構；（4）相同的音高類別在不同樂章中獲得不同的上下文身份，類似於自然語言處理中的上下文與靜態嵌入——而無監督聚類在沒有音樂理論輸入的情況下恢復了調性結構。我們構建了一個反向聲音化（將分析特徵解碼回MIDI），並量化編碼-解碼循環的手性：什麼分佈被保留，什麼序列排序被摧毀。受到聽眾觀察到解碼的作品聽起來像“無法重疊的鏡像異構體”的啟發，手性測量顯示重建損失隨著n-gram順序單調增加。自助基準和子樣本檢查確認所有樂章攜帶的序列信息超過噪音，儘管原始值受樣本大小的影響。跨領域比較顯示，自然語言的手性高於音樂，反映出更強的序列約束。

##### **Expert-Driven Survival Machines: Improving Stratification and Interpretability in Multiple Clinical Cohorts**
2606.14608v1 by Farica Zhuang, Zixuan Wen, Christos Davatzikos, Li Shen

Survival prediction plays a central role for healthcare providers and clinical researchers. Accurate risk stratification enables early intervention and improved patient management. Most existing deep survival models learn one common feature representation for all patients, which may hide important differences between patient subgroups. In contrast, a Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) framework allows different parts of the model to focus on different patient patterns, leading to more individualized representations. Therefore, in this work, we propose a mixture-of-experts enhanced adaptive deep clustering survival framework (AdaCSM) for modeling such heterogeneous survival patterns. We introduce a routing-based expert mechanism that enables conditional specialization within a parametric survival modeling framework. The proposed architecture allocates patients to specialized risk predictors dynamically while preserving the patient survival and subtype clustering objectives. We compare our method with state-of-the-art survival and deep clustering models on multiple real-world longitudinal clinical cohorts spanning diverse disease domains. The proposed method demonstrates improved predictive performance and leads to interpretable results in survival analysis.

摘要：生存預測在醫療提供者和臨床研究人員中扮演著核心角色。準確的風險分層使得早期介入和改善病人管理成為可能。大多數現有的深度生存模型為所有病人學習一個共同的特徵表示，這可能隱藏了病人子群之間的重要差異。相對而言，混合專家（MoE）框架允許模型的不同部分專注於不同的病人模式，從而導致更個性化的表示。因此，在本研究中，我們提出了一種基於混合專家的增強自適應深度聚類生存框架（AdaCSM），用於建模這種異質的生存模式。我們引入了一種基於路由的專家機制，使得在參數生存建模框架內實現條件專業化。所提出的架構動態地將病人分配給專門的風險預測器，同時保留病人的生存和亞型聚類目標。我們將我們的方法與多個現實世界的長期臨床隊列中的最先進生存和深度聚類模型進行比較，這些隊列涵蓋了多種疾病領域。所提出的方法顯示出改進的預測性能，並在生存分析中導致可解釋的結果。

##### **A Comparative Study of Deep Learning Architectures for Multi-Horizon Behavioural Forecasting for Mobile Health**
2606.14604v1 by Pavlos Nicolaou, Kleanthis Malialis, Artemis Kontou, Panayiotis Kolios

Wearable devices and smartphones generate rich behavioural time series that can support proactive health interventions, yet systematic comparisons of modern forecasting architectures for these data are lacking. In particular, it remains unclear how models generalise across populations, how different architectures respond to participant-level fine-tuning and how forecasting accuracy degrades across multi-day horizons. We benchmark six deep learning architectures, two zero-shot Foundation Models (FM) and statistical baselines on three public datasets encompassing over 800 participants, reporting per-feature metrics for step counts, screen time and sleep duration across 1-8 day horizons. We further conduct a per-feature personalisation study across all six architectures and assess FM transferability across dataset sizes and temporal granularities. Our key findings are: (i) no single architecture dominates, PatchTST leads among trained models while the three runners-up (TCN, MLP, Transformer) show no meaningful performance difference; (ii) the FM TimesFM matches or exceeds trained models zero-shot, especially in low-data regimes and (iii) participant-level fine-tuning reduces per-feature RMSE by 16-60\%, with sleep benefiting most and step counts least. These results provide practical guidance on architecture selection, FM applicability and personalisation strategies for mobile health forecasting. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first study to jointly evaluate modern deep learning, FMs and personalisation for multi-horizon behavioural forecasting from wearables.

##### **LoSoNA: A Benchmark for Local Social Norm Adaptation in Group Conversations**
2606.14600v1 by Mateusz Winiarek, Maksymilian Bilski, Mateusz Jacniacki

Online group chats are social spaces with local conversational norms that are rarely stated explicitly. The ability and willingness of LLM-based agents to recognize and adapt to these norms remains mostly unexplored. We introduce LoSoNA, a benchmark for local social norm adaptation in multi-party chat. Each scenario gives a subject model a curated group-chat transcript in which non-subject participants demonstrate a hidden local norm, followed by a final elicitor turn that forces a response revealing whether the subject has inferred that norm. We evaluate eight frontier and open-weight models under four prompting conditions that vary how explicitly the model is told to treat the prior conversation as evidence for how it should answer. Naive prompting remains limited for most models; explicit norm-aware prompting helps unevenly, with Gemini 3.1 Pro reaching $84.2\%$ and Claude Fable 5 reaching $81.6\%$, while several other models show small gains or regressions. LoSoNA contributes to recent calls for evaluating LLM social capabilities by testing whether models can infer local conversational norms from precedent and use them in a one-turn group-chat response.
