##### **DIFF-ERO: A Conformance-Aware Loss for Deep Learning in Process Mining**
2606.14283v1 by Johannes De Smedt, Jari Peeperkorn, Artem Polyvyanyy, Jochen De Weerdt

Deep learning has driven many recent advances in process analytics, especially for predictive and prescriptive monitoring. However, standard objectives such as cross-entropy optimize local next-step likelihoods and only implicitly capture control-flow structure. As a result, models can achieve high token-level accuracy while permitting imprecise global behaviour. We introduce DIFF-ERO, a conformance-aware loss function for deep learning models on process data. DIFF-ERO is a differentiable formulation of entropy-based stochastic conformance that incorporates control-flow information during training. Our approach constructs batch-level stochastic transition matrices with soft edge memberships, allowing structural precision and recall signals to directly inform backpropagation. The loss is model-agnostic and can be applied whenever the final representation parametrizes stochastic transitions. We instantiate DIFF-ERO in transformer encoder-decoder pipelines for next-activity prediction and use it jointly with cross-entropy to analyse its theoretical components with respect to convergence. Across benchmarks comparing other loss functions and targets, DIFF-ERO shows improved predictive performance where structure matters most while maintaining parity elsewhere. At the same time, the learned stochastic automaton converges towards the structural ground truth, indicating that the network internalizes process model structure.

摘要：深度學習推動了過程分析的許多近期進展，特別是在預測和處方監控方面。<lb/>然而，標準目標如交叉熵優化局部下一步的可能性，並且僅隱式捕捉控制流結構。<lb/>因此，模型可以在允許不精確的全局行為的同時實現高的標記級準確性。<lb/>我們引入了DIFF-ERO，一種針對過程數據的深度學習模型的符合度感知損失函數。<lb/>DIFF-ERO是一種可微分的基於熵的隨機符合度的公式，並在訓練過程中納入控制流信息。<lb/>我們的方法構建了具有軟邊緣成員資格的批量級隨機轉移矩陣，允許結構精度和召回信號直接告知反向傳播。<lb/>該損失函數與模型無關，並且可以在最終表示參數化隨機轉移時應用。<lb/>我們在Transformer編碼器-解碼器管道中實現了DIFF-ERO，用於下一活動預測，並將其與交叉熵共同使用，以分析其理論組成部分與收斂的關係。<lb/>在比較其他損失函數和目標的基準測試中，DIFF-ERO在結構最重要的地方顯示出改進的預測性能，同時在其他地方保持平衡。<lb/>與此同時，學習到的隨機自動機向結構的真實情況收斂，這表明網絡內化了過程模型結構。

##### **Does the Judge Prefer English? Evaluating Language-Switching Invariance in LLM-as-a-Judge**
2606.14278v1 by Shaojie Yin

Large language models (LLMs) are now widely used as automatic judges for open-ended instruction-following evaluation. This practice is convenient, scalable, and often more semantically aware than reference-based metrics, but it also introduces a new reliability question: does a judge evaluate the quality of an answer, or does it also react to the language in which the comparison is presented? We propose Judge-LS, a lightweight meta-evaluation protocol that transforms LLMBar response-pair items into English, Chinese, and Chinese-English language-switched variants. A reliable judge should preserve its preference under label-preserving language transformations and should not prefer a language when two answers are translation-equivalent. We evaluate four API-accessible judges on the full 419-item LLMBar benchmark, producing 13,408 successful pairwise judgments. Across models, Chinese and language-switched presentations induce 10.7--14.4% preference flips relative to English, and all judges achieve their highest accuracy in English. However, translation-equivalent tie probes do not reveal a systematic English preference: most probes are judged as ties, and non-tie decisions more often favor Chinese. We add confidence intervals, paired significance tests, and an automatic transformation audit with a sensitivity analysis that excludes mechanically flagged high-risk variants. The experiment requires no model training, uses only API calls, and is feasible on modest local hardware.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）現在被廣泛用作開放式指令跟隨評估的自動評審。<lb/>這種做法方便、可擴展，並且通常比基於參考的指標更具語義意識，但它也引入了一個新的可靠性問題：評審是評估答案的質量，還是也會對比較所呈現的語言作出反應？<lb/>我們提出了Judge-LS，一種輕量級的元評估協議，它將LLMBar的回應對項目轉換為英語、中文和中英語切換變體。<lb/>一個可靠的評審應該在保留標籤的語言轉換下保持其偏好，並且在兩個答案是翻譯等價時不應偏好某一語言。<lb/>我們在完整的419項LLMBar基準上評估了四個可通過API訪問的評審，產生了13,408個成功的成對判斷。<lb/>在各模型中，中文和語言切換的呈現相對於英語引起了10.7--14.4%的偏好翻轉，所有評審在英語中的準確性最高。<lb/>然而，翻譯等價的平局探測並未顯示出系統性的英語偏好：大多數探測被判定為平局，而非平局的決策則更常偏向中文。<lb/>我們添加了置信區間、成對顯著性檢驗，以及一個自動轉換審計，並進行了敏感性分析，排除了機械標記的高風險變體。<lb/>這項實驗不需要模型訓練，只使用API調用，並且在適度的本地硬體上可行。

##### **ScoreGate: Adaptive Chunk Selection for Retrieval-Augmented Generation via Dual-Score Statistical Fusion**
2606.14269v1 by Karamvir Singh, Arvind Jain

Fixed-cardinality retrieval injects a constant top-K chunks into the generator regardless of query complexity, causing over-retrieval for narrow queries and under-retrieval for compositional ones. We describe ScoreGate, a lightweight score-space decision mechanism that controls retrieval cardinality at inference time using two scores already produced by the standard pipeline: bi-encoder similarity s_i and cross-encoder reranker score r_i, with no additional model inference calls required. Its core insight is that cross-encoder affirmation can rescue semantically relevant chunks that bi-encoder retrieval ranks poorly due to vocabulary mismatch -- a failure mode unaddressed by fixed-K or single-score thresholding. On MS MARCO (200 dev queries), ScoreGate achieves MRR@10 = 0.401 with 35% fewer retained chunks than Standard Top-K. On an internal benchmark (n=300, Fleiss' kappa=0.87), ScoreGate observed zero false positives (95% CI [96.4%, 100%]) at 97.77-99.34% recall, with 34.8% fewer tokens per query and only 31ms added latency. Results on both MS MARCO and real-world production traffic suggest that adaptive retrieval cardinality can improve retrieval efficiency without degrading retrieval quality.

摘要：固定基數檢索無論查詢複雜性如何，都會將一個固定的前K個區塊注入生成器，這導致對於狹窄查詢的過度檢索以及對於組合查詢的不足檢索。我們描述了ScoreGate，一種輕量級的分數空間決策機制，該機制在推理時使用標準管道已產生的兩個分數來控制檢索基數：雙編碼器相似度s_i和交叉編碼器重排序分數r_i，無需額外的模型推理調用。其核心見解是，交叉編碼器的肯定可以挽救由於詞彙不匹配而被雙編碼器檢索排名較低的語義相關區塊——這是一種固定K或單一分數閾值未能解決的失效模式。在MS MARCO（200個開發查詢）上，ScoreGate達到了MRR@10 = 0.401，保留的區塊比標準Top-K少35%。在一個內部基準測試（n=300，Fleiss' kappa=0.87）中，ScoreGate觀察到零假陽性（95% CI [96.4%, 100%]），在97.77-99.34%的召回率下，每個查詢的標記數少了34.8%，且僅增加了31毫秒的延遲。MS MARCO和真實世界生產流量的結果表明，自適應檢索基數可以提高檢索效率，而不降低檢索質量。

##### **The Linguistics Olympiads: Towards a New Corpus for Linguistics Research?**
2606.14257v1 by Vlad A. Neacsu

Linguistics olympiad problems (LOPs) are a category of self-sufficient puzzles consisting of a scaled-down corpus representative of certain linguistic phenomena, from which the solver must deduce a primitive set of rules of the language and then translate a new set of elements. The linguistics olympiads (LOs) have become a worldwide phenomenon with 43 different territories taking part in the International Linguistics Olympiad (IOL) 2025. While the typology and solving strategies of LOPs have been analysed, their scientific facet and connections to academic linguistics have yet to be explored. LOPs are directly connected to many linguistic fields, e.g., linguistic typology, linguistic relativity, and linguistics fieldwork. Recently, LOPs have become a research focus as benchmarks for large language models, thus highlighting their usefulness in computational linguistics. Nevertheless, they have not yet been integrated into mainstream linguistics research. This paper attempts to open new directions of including this particular type of puzzle in academic research by offering a structured evaluation of LOPs as linguistic data sources and proposes criteria for their responsible use in academic research. Starting from a set of over 1800 LOPs, this study critically examines the potential of LOPs as a novel corpus for linguistics research by discussing their strengths and limitations as tools, as well as the areas of linguistics into which these problems could fit. This work forms the foundation for a broader initiative aimed at bridging the gap between LOs and academic linguistics, by establishing a robust theoretical framework for LOPs.

摘要：語言學奧林匹克問題（LOPs）是一類自給自足的謎題，由縮小的語料庫組成，代表某些語言現象，解題者必須從中推導出語言的基本規則集，然後翻譯出一組新的元素。語言學奧林匹克（LOs）已成為全球現象，43個不同地區參加了2025年國際語言學奧林匹克（IOL）。雖然LOPs的類型和解題策略已被分析，但其科學面向和與學術語言學的聯繫尚未被探討。LOPs與許多語言學領域直接相關，例如語言類型學、語言相對論和語言學田野調查。最近，LOPs已成為大型語言模型的基準研究焦點，從而突顯了它們在計算語言學中的實用性。然而，它們尚未被整合進主流的語言學研究中。本文試圖通過提供LOPs作為語言數據來源的結構化評估，開辟將這種特定類型的謎題納入學術研究的新方向，並提出其在學術研究中負責任使用的標準。從超過1800個LOPs的集合開始，本研究批判性地檢視LOPs作為語言學研究新語料庫的潛力，討論其作為工具的優勢和局限性，以及這些問題可能適合的語言學領域。這項工作為一個更廣泛的倡議奠定了基礎，旨在縮小LOs與學術語言學之間的鴻溝，通過建立LOPs的堅實理論框架。

##### **HarnessX: A Composable, Adaptive, and Evolvable Agent Harness Foundry**
2606.14249v1 by Tingyang Chen, Shuo Lu, Kang Zhao, Weicheng Meng, Hanlin Teng, Tianhao Li, Chao Li, Xule Liu, Jian Liang, Zhizhong Zhang, Yuan Xie, Heng Qu, Kun Shao, Jian Luan

AI agent performance depends critically on the runtime harness, comprising the prompts, tools, memory, and control flow that mediate how a model observes, reasons, and acts. Yet today's harnesses remain largely hand-crafted and static: each new model or task still demands bespoke scaffolding, and the rich traces produced during execution are rarely distilled back into systematic improvement. We introduce HarnessX, a foundry for composable, adaptive, and evolvable agent harnesses. HarnessX assembles typed harness primitives via a substitution algebra, adapts them through AEGIS, a trace-driven multi-agent evolution engine grounded in an operational mirror between symbolic adaptation and reinforcement learning, and closes the harness-model loop by turning trajectories into both harness updates and model training signal. Across five benchmarks (ALFWorld, GAIA, WebShop, tau^3-Bench, and SWE-bench Verified), HarnessX yields an average gain of +14.5% (up to +44.0%), with gains largest where baselines are lowest. These results suggest that agent progress need not come from model scaling alone: composing and evolving runtime interfaces from execution feedback is an actionable and complementary lever. The complete codebase will be open-sourced in a future release.

摘要：AI 代理的性能在很大程度上依賴於運行時的框架，其中包括提示、工具、記憶體和控制流程，這些因素調節模型如何觀察、推理和行動。<lb/>然而，當前的框架仍然主要是手工製作和靜態的：每個新模型或任務仍然需要量身定制的支架，而在執行過程中產生的豐富痕跡很少被提煉回系統性的改進中。<lb/>我們介紹 HarnessX，一個可組合、可適應和可演變的代理框架的鑄造廠。<lb/>HarnessX 通過替代代數組裝類型化的框架原語，通過 AEGIS 進行適應，AEGIS 是一個基於符號適應和強化學習之間操作鏡像的追蹤驅動多代理演化引擎，並通過將軌跡轉化為框架更新和模型訓練信號來關閉框架-模型的循環。<lb/>在五個基準測試（ALFWorld、GAIA、WebShop、tau^3-Bench 和 SWE-bench Verified）中，HarnessX 平均獲得 +14.5% 的增益（最高可達 +44.0%），增益在基線最低的地方最大。<lb/>這些結果表明，代理的進展不必僅來自模型的擴展：從執行反饋中組合和演變運行時介面是一個可行且互補的槓桿。<lb/>完整的代碼庫將在未來的版本中開源。

##### **Decoupled Mixture-of-Experts for Parametric Knowledge Injection**
2606.14243v1 by Baoqing Yue, Weihang Su, Qingyao Ai, Yichen Tang, Changyue Wang, Jiacheng Kang, Jingtao Zhan, Yiqun Liu

Knowledge injection aims to equip large language models (LLMs) with external, domain-specific, or time-sensitive knowledge. Existing approaches typically face a trade-off between flexibility and integration: retrieval-augmented generation keeps knowledge outside the model but only provides prompt-level augmentation, whereas post-training based methods encode new knowledge into shared parameters but may introduce catastrophic forgetting, knowledge conflict, and costly updates. In this paper, we propose Decoupled Mixture-of-Experts (DMoE), a modular architecture for parametric knowledge injection that decouples both experts and the router from the base model. DMoE converts external knowledge corpora into independently updatable expert modules and uses a lightweight uncertainty-aware router to activate relevant experts only when the base model lacks sufficient knowledge during generation. To support efficient auto-regressive inference, DMoE attaches experts only to the final-layer feed-forward network, preserving KV-cache reuse while enabling parameter-level knowledge augmentation. Experiments on knowledge-intensive benchmarks show that DMoE consistently improves answer quality over retrieval and adapter-based baselines.

摘要：知識注入旨在為大型語言模型（LLMs）提供外部、特定領域或時間敏感的知識。現有的方法通常面臨靈活性和整合之間的權衡：檢索增強生成將知識保持在模型之外，但僅提供提示級別的增強，而基於後訓練的方法則將新知識編碼到共享參數中，但可能引入災難性遺忘、知識衝突和高成本的更新。在本文中，我們提出了解耦混合專家（DMoE），這是一種參數化知識注入的模組化架構，將專家和路由器與基礎模型解耦。DMoE 將外部知識語料庫轉換為可獨立更新的專家模組，並使用輕量級的不確定性感知路由器，僅在基礎模型在生成過程中缺乏足夠知識時啟用相關專家。為了支持高效的自回歸推理，DMoE 僅將專家附加到最終層的前饋網絡，保留 KV 緩存重用，同時實現參數級別的知識增強。在知識密集型基準測試中的實驗顯示，DMoE 在答案質量上始終優於基於檢索和適配器的基準。

##### **AFFORDANCE20Q: Evaluating Affordance Reasoning from Physical Properties**
2606.14240v1 by Yifan Jiang, Meige Yang, Zitong Li, Jay Pujara

Affordance reasoning, the inference of an object's action possibilities from its physical properties (e.g., shape and material), is fundamental to human physical understanding and increasingly critical for Large Language Models (LLMs). However, existing affordance benchmarks largely expose explicit object identities in the evaluation setup, allowing models to rely on memorized object-affordance mappings rather than reasoning over physical properties. To address this gap, we introduce Affordance20Q, a novel affordance reasoning benchmark formulated as a 20-Questions game without exposing the object's identity. In each game, the model identifies a hidden object's affordance from a candidate set by asking yes/no questions about its physical properties. Affordance20Q comprises 1,009 games over 454 objects and 59 affordances, all manually filtered, refined, and annotated. We conduct comprehensive experiments with 15 state-of-the-art LLMs and find a substantial gap (~20 points) compared to human performance. A KL-based information-gain (IG) analysis further shows that models fail to ask discriminating questions as the game progresses. To close the gap, we develop KB-Anchored Rule Induction (KARI), a pipeline based on LLMs that generates affordance rules grounded in evidence from knowledge bases (KBs). KARI improves open-source LLMs by up to 15.2 points, while the limited coverage of KBs hinders further gains. We release all our code and data at https://github.com/1171-jpg/Affordance20Q.git

摘要：可供性推理，即從物體的物理特性（例如形狀和材料）推斷其行動可能性，對於人類的物理理解至關重要，並且對於大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越重要。然而，現有的可供性基準在評估設置中大多暴露了明確的物體身份，使模型能夠依賴於記憶中的物體-可供性映射，而不是對物理特性進行推理。為了解決這一差距，我們引入了Affordance20Q，這是一個新穎的可供性推理基準，形式為一個不暴露物體身份的20問遊戲。在每個遊戲中，模型通過詢問有關物體物理特性的是/否問題來識別隱藏物體的可供性。Affordance20Q包含1,009個遊戲，涵蓋454個物體和59種可供性，所有遊戲均經過手動篩選、精煉和註釋。我們對15個最先進的LLMs進行了全面實驗，發現與人類表現相比存在顯著差距（約20分）。基於KL的信息增益（IG）分析進一步顯示，隨著遊戲的進展，模型未能提出具有區分性的問題。為了縮小這一差距，我們開發了基於知識庫（KB）的規則歸納（KARI），這是一個基於LLMs的流程，生成基於知識庫證據的可供性規則。KARI使開源LLMs的表現提高了最多15.2分，而知識庫的有限覆蓋則阻礙了進一步的提升。我們在https://github.com/1171-jpg/Affordance20Q.git上發布了我們的所有代碼和數據。

##### **SkillAudit: Ground-Truth-Free Skill Evolution via Paired Trajectory Auditing**
2606.14239v1 by Haowen Gao, Haoran Chen, Can Wang, Shasha Guo, Liang Pang, Zhaoyang Liu, Huawei Shen, Xueqi Cheng

Agent skills are structured procedural packages that guide frozen LLM agents in specialized workflows. Skills rarely remain sufficient after deployment: edge cases, API changes, and deployment constraints become visible only through use, making skill evolution a practical necessity. Existing methods depend on privileged feedback such as held-out validation scores, hidden test outcomes, or environment rewards -- signals often unavailable when a practitioner has only a task description and workspace data. We introduce SkillAudit, a framework for evolving agent skills without ground-truth feedback. The key idea is paired trajectory auditing: at each iteration, the same task is executed with and without the candidate skill, isolating how the skill changes agent behavior without external labels. To turn behavioral differences into edit guidance, SkillAudit uses Process-Aligned Contrastive Evaluation (PACE), a cluster of evaluators that maps trajectory divergences to diagnostic signals linked to specific passages in the skill document. A structural verifier, compiled once from the task specification and then fixed, checks task constraints and rolls back harmful updates. SkillAudit routes edits through two pipelines: Refine removes noisy or irrelevant guidance from broadly useful skills, while Repair replaces passages that conflict with the task. Across 89 containerized tasks spanning 8 professional domains, SkillAudit achieves 73.9% average task reward, outperforming an agent without skills (40.9%) and the static expert skill (56.7%). These gains are obtained without accessing hidden tests, reference solutions, or external scoring functions during evolution.

摘要：代理技能是結構化的程序包，指導凍結的LLM代理在專業工作流程中運作。技能在部署後很少保持足夠：邊緣案例、API變更和部署限制只有在使用過程中才能顯現，使得技能演進成為一種實際的必要性。現有方法依賴於特權反饋，例如保留的驗證分數、隱藏的測試結果或環境獎勵——這些信號在從業者僅擁有任務描述和工作空間數據時往往無法獲得。我們介紹了SkillAudit，一個在沒有真實反饋的情況下演進代理技能的框架。關鍵思想是配對軌跡審核：在每次迭代中，執行相同的任務，分別使用和不使用候選技能，從而孤立出技能如何改變代理行為，而不需要外部標籤。為了將行為差異轉化為編輯指導，SkillAudit使用過程對齊對比評估（PACE），這是一組評估者，將軌跡偏差映射到與技能文檔中特定段落相關的診斷信號。結構驗證器從任務規範中編譯一次後固定，檢查任務約束並回滾有害的更新。SkillAudit通過兩個管道路由編輯：Refine移除來自廣泛有用技能的噪聲或不相關的指導，而Repair則替換與任務衝突的段落。在涵蓋8個專業領域的89個容器化任務中，SkillAudit實現了73.9%的平均任務獎勵，超越了沒有技能的代理（40.9%）和靜態專家技能（56.7%）。這些增益是在演進過程中未接觸隱藏測試、參考解決方案或外部評分函數的情況下獲得的。

##### **When and How Severely: Scenario-Specific Safety Envelopes for Driving VLAs**
2606.14238v1 by Abhinaw Priyadershi, Jelena Frtunikj

Safety certification of Vision-Language-Action (VLA) driving planners under ISO 21448 (SOTIF) rests on an Operational Design Domain (ODD) specification that answers two complementary questions: when does the planner start to fail, and how severely does it fail once it does? We evaluate Alpamayo R1, a 10B-parameter open-weight driving VLA, on 15,968 (clip, attack) pairs. We find a conservative-aggregate gap: an aggregate safe threshold of $σ\leq 50$ under a 15% average displacement error (ADE) budget masks well-sampled scenarios that tolerate the top of the tested grid ($σ= 70$). A Gaussian Mixture Model (GMM) on the changed-explanation subset identifies six discrete severity bands (BIC-optimal $k{=}6$), so two perturbation conditions with the same mean error can differ materially in their share of high-severity (C4/C5) failures. Joining the two analyses on the same corpus surfaces a finding neither yields in isolation: the scenarios with the loosest noise thresholds are not those with the lowest high-severity rate: STOP_SIGNAL concentrates roughly $4\times$ the C4/C5 share of LANE_KEEPING despite tolerating a larger $σ$. A deployable SOTIF ODD specification for driving VLAs therefore requires a two-dimensional safety envelope, not a single aggregate value per hazard.

摘要：安全認證的視覺-語言-行動 (VLA) 駕駛規劃者根據 ISO 21448 (SOTIF) 的標準，依賴於一個操作設計範疇 (ODD) 規範，該規範回答了兩個互補的問題：規劃者何時開始失效，以及一旦失效，其失效程度有多嚴重？我們在 15,968 個 (clip, attack) 配對上評估了 Alpamayo R1，一個具有 10B 參數的開放權重駕駛 VLA。我們發現了一個保守的總體差距：在 15% 的平均位移誤差 (ADE) 預算下，$σ\leq 50$ 的總體安全閾值掩蓋了那些能夠容忍測試網格頂部 ($σ= 70$) 的良好取樣場景。對變更解釋子集進行的高斯混合模型 (GMM) 識別出六個離散的嚴重程度帶 (BIC 最優 $k{=}6$)，因此兩個具有相同平均誤差的擾動條件在高嚴重性 (C4/C5) 失效的比例上可能有實質差異。將兩個分析結合在同一語料庫上，顯示出一個單獨進行時都無法得出的發現：噪聲閾值最寬鬆的場景並不是高嚴重性失效率最低的場景：STOP_SIGNAL 的 C4/C5 份額大約是 LANE_KEEPING 的 $4\times$，儘管容忍了更大的 $σ$。因此，駕駛 VLA 的可部署 SOTIF ODD 規範需要一個二維安全包絡，而不是每個危害的一個單一總體值。

##### **A Multi-Domain Feature Fusion Framework for Generalizable Deepfake Detection Across Different Generators**
2606.14230v1 by Amna Amjid, Sana Qadir, Mehwish Fatima, Raja Khurram Shahzad

Deepfakes are artificially generated images, audio, or videos that threaten privacy, security, and information integrity. Detecting such content is crucial for countering disinformation, as the latest models generate highly realistic content. While spatial- or frequency-based approaches achieve good detection rates on Generative Adversarial Networks (GANs)-based generated deepfakes, they often struggle with recent diffusion model-generated images. In particular, existing approaches rarely exploit complementary multi-domain representations or systematically evaluate cross-generator robustness. To address these challenges, we propose a multi-domain deepfake detection framework called SGFF-Net (Spatial-Gradient-Frequency Fusion Network) that integrates spatial, gradient, and DWT (Discrete Wavelet Transform)-based frequency representations within a dual residual learning architecture. Experimental results show that the SGFF-Net achieves 98.95\% accuracy in intra-dataset evaluation and improves performance in both cross-model (70.46\%) and cross-paradigm (69.94\%) settings. Incorporating multi-source training and data augmentation further enhances robustness, increasing accuracy from 70.46\% to 79.80\% in cross-model evaluation, from 69\% to 78\% in cross-paradigm evaluation, and from 61.50\% to 75.80\% on real-world data. Unlike single-domain detectors, the SGFF-Net learns complementary forensic cues across spatial, gradient, and wavelet-frequency domains, resulting in greater robustness under cross-generator and cross-paradigm evaluation. The results further show that combining multi-domain representations with data diversity and augmentation substantially improves generalization, providing practical insights for developing more reliable deepfake detection systems.

摘要：深偽影像是人工生成的圖像、音頻或視頻，威脅到隱私、安全和信息完整性。檢測這類內容對於對抗虛假信息至關重要，因為最新的模型生成的內容非常逼真。雖然基於空間或頻率的方法在生成對抗網絡（GANs）生成的深偽影像上達到了良好的檢測率，但它們在處理最近的擴散模型生成的圖像時常常遇到困難。特別是，現有的方法很少利用互補的多域表示或系統性評估跨生成器的穩健性。為了解決這些挑戰，我們提出了一個名為SGFF-Net（空間-梯度-頻率融合網絡）的多域深偽影像檢測框架，該框架在雙殘差學習架構中整合了空間、梯度和基於離散小波變換（DWT）的頻率表示。實驗結果顯示，SGFF-Net在內部數據集評估中達到了98.95\%的準確率，並在跨模型（70.46\%）和跨範式（69.94\%）設置中提高了性能。結合多源訓練和數據增強進一步增強了穩健性，將跨模型評估的準確率從70.46\%提高到79.80\%，跨範式評估的準確率從69\%提高到78\%，在真實世界數據上的準確率從61.50\%提高到75.80\%。與單域檢測器不同，SGFF-Net在空間、梯度和小波頻率域之間學習互補的取證線索，從而在跨生成器和跨範式評估中實現了更大的穩健性。結果進一步顯示，將多域表示與數據多樣性和增強相結合顯著提高了泛化能力，為開發更可靠的深偽影像檢測系統提供了實用的見解。

##### **Closing the Reflection Gap: A Free Calibration Bonus for Agentic RL**
2606.14211v1 by Yinglun Zhu

LLMs are increasingly deployed as agents that interact with external environments and observe feedback such as execution results, error messages, and tool outputs. A well-functioning agent should be able to leverage this feedback to accurately assess its own performance. Yet we find a persistent reflection gap: LLM agents tend to mis-assess their own outputs after observing concrete environment feedback -- even for questions they correctly answered -- and standard RL barely helps due to a credit-assignment mismatch. To close this gap, we propose RefGRPO, a simple yet effective fix that augments standard RL algorithms with two key ingredients: a free calibration bonus computed by contrasting the agent's own reflection with the actual outcome (requiring no additional reward model, LLM judge, or external annotation), and a dynamic schedule on its coefficient. Compared to standard RL baselines, our method simultaneously improves reflection calibration (e.g., reduces underconfidence rate $44.4\% \to 7.7\%$) and task accuracy (e.g., $75.1\% \to 76.5\%$) on text-to-SQL across five benchmarks. The resulting calibrated reflection turns the agent into its own verifier grounded in environment feedback, which further enables (i) better self-improvement that uses reflections as pseudo-rewards without outcome supervision, and (ii) more effective test-time selective prediction by committing only to rollouts flagged as correct.

摘要：LLMs 正在越來越多地被用作與外部環境互動並觀察反饋（例如執行結果、錯誤信息和工具輸出）的代理。<lb/>一個運作良好的代理應該能夠利用這些反饋準確評估自己的表現。<lb/>然而，我們發現存在一個持續的反思差距：LLM 代理在觀察到具體環境反饋後，往往會錯誤評估自己的輸出——即使是對於他們正確回答的問題——而標準強化學習幾乎無法幫助，因為存在信用分配不匹配。<lb/>為了縮小這個差距，我們提出了 RefGRPO，一種簡單但有效的修正方法，它通過兩個關鍵成分增強標準強化學習算法：一個通過將代理的自我反思與實際結果進行對比計算的免費校準獎勵（不需要額外的獎勵模型、LLM 評判或外部註釋），以及其係數的動態調整計劃。<lb/>與標準強化學習基準相比，我們的方法同時改善了反思校準（例如，將低自信率從 $44.4\% \to 7.7\%$ 降低）和任務準確性（例如，$75.1\% \to 76.5\%$）在五個基準上的文本到 SQL 的表現。<lb/>結果，經過校準的反思使代理成為基於環境反饋的自我驗證者，進一步實現了（i）更好的自我改進，利用反思作為偽獎勵而不需要結果監督，以及（ii）更有效的測試時選擇性預測，僅對標記為正確的回合進行承諾。

##### **From Prompts to Responses: Dual-Sided Data Leakage and Defense in Split Large Language Models**
2606.14210v1 by Zixuan Gu, Xiaojun Ye, Yang Liu

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in privacy-sensitive domains, where users must balance the risk of data exposure through external APIs against the high computational cost of local deployment. Split learning has therefore emerged as a promising paradigm for LLM fine-tuning and inference under limited local resources. However, it introduces new privacy risks. Prior work primarily studies leakage of private input prompts, typically via inversion attacks on intermediate representations, while the potential for sensitive information leakage through generative response outputs remains largely unexplored.
  In this work, we unveil novel vulnerabilities of Split-LLM by presenting Patched Model Inversion with Dual-Sided Initialization (PIDI), a two-stage attack that simultaneously targets both private input prompts and output responses in Split-LLM settings. It combines dual-sided initialization with a patched inversion strategy to tackle long sequences, substantially outperforming prior inversion methods. To counter threats from both sides, we further propose the Adapter-based DualGuard with Mutual Information Defense (ADMI), which integrates an adapter-based local warmup strategy and mutual information regularization to provide a strong empirical privacy protection with minimal impact on task performance. Extensive experiments across diverse tasks and models demonstrate that ADMI effectively defends against PIDI and other state-of-the-art inversion attacks. Our code is publicly available at https://github.com/FLAIR-THU/VFLAIR-LLM.

摘要：大型語言模型 (LLMs) 正在越來越多地應用於隱私敏感的領域，在這些領域中，使用者必須在通過外部 API 暴露數據的風險與本地部署的高計算成本之間取得平衡。因此，分割學習作為一種有前景的範式出現，適用於在有限的本地資源下進行 LLM 的微調和推理。然而，它也帶來了新的隱私風險。先前的研究主要集中於私有輸入提示的洩漏，通常是通過對中間表示的反演攻擊，而通過生成響應輸出洩漏敏感信息的潛力仍然在很大程度上未被探索。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們揭示了 Split-LLM 的新漏洞，提出了具有雙面初始化的修補模型反演 (PIDI)，這是一種兩階段攻擊，同時針對 Split-LLM 設置中的私有輸入提示和輸出響應。它結合了雙面初始化和修補反演策略，以應對長序列，顯著超越了先前的反演方法。為了對抗來自兩側的威脅，我們進一步提出了基於適配器的雙重防護與互信息防禦 (ADMI)，它集成了基於適配器的本地預熱策略和互信息正則化，以在對任務性能影響最小的情況下提供強大的實證隱私保護。對各種任務和模型的廣泛實驗表明，ADMI 有效防禦 PIDI 和其他最先進的反演攻擊。我們的代碼在 https://github.com/FLAIR-THU/VFLAIR-LLM 上公開可用。

##### **Detecting undisclosed LLM-generated content in parliamentary texts**
2606.14209v1 by Minerva Suvanto, Andrea McGlinchey, Peter J. Barclay, Mattias Wahde

In this paper, we evaluate the extent of undisclosed LLM-generated content in texts from the parliaments of the United Kingdom and Sweden. In many areas, such as in journalism or in academic writing, there are often requirements to clearly disclose whether AI tools, such as LLMs, have been used. In the case of parliamentary texts, the guidelines on disclosure of AI use are more vague. However, in order to maintain transparency and retain public trust, it is generally recommended that parliamentarians should state whether or not they have used AI when writing texts, such as parliamentary motions. Here, we train an interpretable (glass-box) text classifier using pre-LLM parliamentary texts and LLM-generated versions of such texts. ##### **MeEvo: Metacognitive Evolution Combined with Natural Evolution for Automatic Heuristic Design**
2606.14202v1 by Zishang Qiu, Xinan Chen, Rong Qu, Ruibin Bai

Large Language Models (LLMs) have advanced Automatic Heuristic Design (AHD) by enabling heuristic generation through reasoning and code synthesis. Existing LLM-based AHD architectures mainly follow two paradigms: Natural Evolution, which uses crossover and mutation to explore heuristic programs, and Metacognitive Evolution, which refines reasoning through reflection. However, Natural Evolution discards reasoning traces, weakening knowledge inheritance and exploitation, while Metacognitive Evolution lacks population-level recombination, limiting exploration and increasing the risk of premature convergence. These limitations reduce search efficiency, stability, and solution quality on complex problems. To address this gap, we propose MeEvo, a dual-layer AHD framework that cyclically couples Natural Evolution and Metacognitive Evolution. Natural Evolution explores heuristic code while recording reasoning traces, fitness values, and errors into a shared history; Metacognitive Evolution then reflects on this history to generate improved heuristics that re-enter the parent pool for the next cycle. This design enables population-driven exploration and reflection-driven refinement to reinforce each other. Experiments on five optimization problems with two LLM backbones show that MeEvo achieves stronger and more stable performance than existing LLM-based AHD architectures, especially on complex constrained tasks.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）透過推理和程式碼合成促進了自動啟發式設計（AHD）的發展。現有的基於LLM的AHD架構主要遵循兩種範式：自然進化，利用交叉和突變來探索啟發式程式，和元認知進化，通過反思來精煉推理。然而，自然進化丟棄推理痕跡，削弱了知識的繼承和利用，而元認知進化則缺乏群體層級的重組，限制了探索並增加了過早收斂的風險。這些限制降低了在複雜問題上的搜索效率、穩定性和解決方案質量。為了解決這一問題，我們提出了MeEvo，一個雙層AHD框架，循環性地結合自然進化和元認知進化。自然進化探索啟發式程式，同時將推理痕跡、適應度值和錯誤記錄到共享歷史中；然後，元認知進化反思這一歷史，以生成改進的啟發式，重新進入父代池以進行下一個循環。這一設計使得基於群體的探索和基於反思的精煉相互強化。在五個優化問題上進行的實驗顯示，MeEvo在性能上比現有的基於LLM的AHD架構更強大且更穩定，特別是在複雜的約束任務上。

##### **When Should Agent Trust Be Conditional? Characterizing and Attacking Skill-Conditional Reputation in Agent Swarms**
2606.14200v1 by Yihan Xia, Taotao Wang

Open platforms increasingly route tasks among heterogeneous LLM agents--differing in base model, scaffold, and tool stack--whose competence varies sharply by skill: an agent excellent at one skill may be useless at another. The standard reputation approach summarizes each agent by a single global trust score, but that scalar is the wrong object here, because routing every task to the globally most-trusted agent leaves the value of specialization unclaimed. We study skill-conditional trust R(i | k)--the trust to place in agent i for a task requiring skill k, rather than one score per agent--and pose three falsifiable questions: when is conditioning worth it, how much cross-skill evidence should be borrowed, and whether that borrowing is safe. A controlled phase-diagram analysis answers the first two: conditional trust wins only in a specific regime--high agent heterogeneity, sparse per-skill evidence, and correlated skills--and the coupling strength beta that buys this data efficiency is dual-use, because the same cross-skill borrowing is also a laundering channel. On a public benchmark of 14 genuinely heterogeneous AppWorld agents, real pools land inside the beneficial regime--a small but genuine gain, with the per-skill best agent genuinely changing across skills. We then show that an attacker with cheap evidence in one skill and none in a target skill hijacks the conditional router, driving routing regret from 0 to 0.94 on a pool our zero-cost Conditional Information Value Test (CIVT) rates GREEN--while the ungated trust verdict it contaminates reads -0.06 instead of the honest +0.19. A zero-evidence gate bounds the attack but does not eliminate it; we characterize the residual cost under an explicit budget. We do not claim Sybil-resistance--we quantify the trade-off.

摘要：開放平台越來越多地在異質的 LLM 代理之間路由任務——這些代理在基礎模型、框架和工具堆疊上各不相同——其能力因技能而異：在某一技能上表現優異的代理在另一技能上可能毫無用處。標準的聲譽方法用單一的全球信任分數來總結每個代理，但這個標量在這裡並不合適，因為將每個任務路由到全球最受信任的代理會使專業化的價值未被利用。我們研究技能條件信任 R(i | k)——對於需要技能 k 的任務，對代理 i 的信任，而不是每個代理一個分數——並提出三個可驗證的問題：何時條件化是值得的，應該借用多少跨技能的證據，以及這種借用是否安全。一個受控的相位圖分析回答了前兩個問題：條件信任僅在特定的範疇內獲勝——高代理異質性、稀疏的每技能證據和相關技能——而購買這種數據效率的耦合強度 beta 是雙重用途的，因為相同的跨技能借用也是一個洗錢渠道。在一個包含 14 個真正異質的 AppWorld 代理的公共基準上，真實的池子落在有利的範疇內——這是一個小但真正的增益，且每技能最佳代理在技能之間確實變化。我們接著顯示，擁有某一技能的廉價證據而在目標技能上沒有證據的攻擊者劫持了條件路由器，將路由遺憾從 0 驟升至 0.94，而我們的零成本條件信息價值測試 (CIVT) 評級為綠色的池子——而它污染的無閘信任判決讀數為 -0.06，而不是誠實的 +0.19。一個零證據閘限制了攻擊但並未消除它；我們在明確預算下描述了剩餘成本。我們不聲稱具備 Sybil 抵抗能力——我們量化了這一權衡。

##### **OdysSim: Building Foundation Models for Human Behavior Simulation**
2606.14199v1 by Xuhui Zhou, Weiwei Sun, Weihua Du, Jiarui Liu, Haojia Sun, Qianou Ma, Tongshuang Wu, Yiming Yang, Maarten Sap

Large language models are increasingly deployed as human simulators for interactive evaluation and social simulation. Yet helpfulness-driven post-training pulls them toward a homogeneous, overly agreeable assistant register, creating a behavioral Sim2Real gap. We present OdysSim, the largest open systematic investigation of behavioral foundation models, i.e., models trained to simulate human behavior at scale. We propose SOUL, a taxonomy of five capability axes (CONV, SS, COG, ROLE, EVAL) that unifies 62 datasets and 23 benchmark tasks under one framework. Specifically, we curate the OdysSim corpus (21.4M interactions, 10B tokens, retrofitted with back-generated social contexts), construct the SOUL-Index benchmark, and develop an end-to-end training recipe combining midtraining, task-specific RL, and expert distillation. The resulting open 8B OSim model ranks first or tied-first on 8 of 23 tasks, outperforming any individual frontier model by this count, with the strongest gains on conversational and social tasks. Its outputs are also more human-like in length, formatting, and word choice, and it transfers zero-shot to out-of-distribution user simulation on $τ$-bench, nearly matching real users on reaction alignment (93.2 vs. 93.5). We further show that LLM-as-judge RL induces reward-hacking patterns, and that our detectors can mitigate them during post-training. Together, our findings suggest that behavioral foundation models require rethinking the LLM training paradigm. We release all artifacts to support future research.

摘要：大型語言模型越來越多地被用作互動評估和社會模擬的人類模擬器。<lb/>然而，以有用性為驅動的後訓練使它們朝著同質化、過於迎合的助手風格發展，造成了行為上的Sim2Real差距。<lb/>我們提出了OdysSim，這是對行為基礎模型進行的最大規模的開放系統性研究，即在大規模上訓練以模擬人類行為的模型。<lb/>我們提出了SOUL，一個包含五個能力軸（CONV、SS、COG、ROLE、EVAL）的分類法，將62個數據集和23個基準任務統一在一個框架下。<lb/>具體而言，我們整理了OdysSim語料庫（2140萬次互動，100億個標記，並重新生成社會背景），構建了SOUL-Index基準，並開發了一個端到端的訓練配方，結合了中期訓練、任務特定的強化學習和專家蒸餾。<lb/>最終的開放8B OSim模型在23個任務中的8個任務上排名第一或並列第一，超越了任何單一的前沿模型，並在對話和社會任務上取得了最強的增長。<lb/>其輸出在長度、格式和用詞上也更接近人類，並且在$τ$-bench上進行零樣本轉移到分佈外的用戶模擬，幾乎在反應一致性上與真實用戶相匹配（93.2對93.5）。<lb/>我們進一步表明，作為評判者的LLM強化學習會引發獎勵黑客模式，而我們的檢測器可以在後訓練期間減輕這些模式。<lb/>總的來說，我們的發現表明，行為基礎模型需要重新思考LLM訓練範式。我們釋放所有工件以支持未來的研究。

##### **Robustness without Wrinkles: Parallel Simulation and Robust MPC for Certified Deformable Manipulation**
2606.14188v1 by Wei-Chen Li, Jeffrey Fang, Sasanka Polisetti, Yuexi Song, Glen Chou

We present CORD-SLS, a real-time control method for safe deformable object manipulation, with a focus on ropes and cloth. At its core is a GPU-parallel differentiable simulator with contact smoothing which enables efficient gradient-based planning through intermittent contact. To robustly satisfy constraints under model and sensing uncertainty, we develop a real-time, GPU-parallel output-feedback robust model predictive control (MPC) algorithm that plans with this simulator. We further show that the simulator accelerates model-based RL for training neural manipulation policies. To improve real-world robustness, we use conformal prediction to calibrate visual-feedback and perception-error bounds for MPC, producing reachable tubes that enable high-probability safe control. We evaluate CORD-SLS on high-dimensional, contact-rich rope and cloth manipulation tasks in simulation and hardware, including obstacle avoidance, routing, folding, and smoothing. Across settings, CORD-SLS achieves millisecond-speed planning, exceeding baselines in safety, speed, and task success.

摘要：我們提出了 CORD-SLS，一種針對安全可變形物體操作的實時控制方法，重點在於繩索和布料。其核心是一個具有接觸平滑功能的 GPU 並行可微分模擬器，該模擬器能夠通過間歇性接觸實現高效的基於梯度的規劃。為了在模型和感測不確定性下穩健地滿足約束，我們開發了一種實時的 GPU 並行輸出反饋穩健模型預測控制 (MPC) 算法，該算法使用這個模擬器進行規劃。我們進一步展示了該模擬器加速了基於模型的強化學習，以訓練神經操作策略。為了提高現實世界的穩健性，我們使用保形預測來校準 MPC 的視覺反饋和感知誤差界限，生成可達的管道，從而實現高概率的安全控制。我們在模擬和硬體上對 CORD-SLS 進行了高維度、接觸豐富的繩索和布料操作任務的評估，包括避障、路由、折疊和平滑。在各種設置中，CORD-SLS 實現了毫秒級的規劃速度，在安全性、速度和任務成功率上超越了基準。

##### **CacheRL:Multi-Turn Tool-Calling Agents via Cached Rollouts and Hybrid Reward**
2606.14179v1 by Md Amirul Islam, Sumiran Thakur, Huancheng Chen, Su Min Park, Jiayun Wang, Gyuhak Kim

We present CacheRL, a system for training small agent foundation models that achieves 92 percent process accuracy on multi-step tool-calling tasks, approaching GPT-5's 94 percent while requiring 100 times less compute. Our approach addresses three challenges in practical agent training: transferring tool-calling knowledge from large models at scale, enabling reinforcement learning without costly live tool execution, and learning robustly from noisy cached environments. CacheRL introduces three key innovations. First, a hybrid thinking trajectory pipeline augments agent trajectories with LLM-generated reasoning traces, producing training examples that teach models not only what tools to call but also why. Second, the CacheAgentLoop eliminates live execution costs through a three-tier fuzzy cache while preserving trajectory fidelity using token-level masking. Third, a cache-tier-aware reward dynamically adjusts answer-quality weights to avoid penalizing models for cache-induced limitations. Through iterative supervised fine-tuning (SFT) and Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), CacheRL improves Qwen3-4B-Thinking's validation reward from 0.43 to 0.78. On public agentic tool-calling benchmarks, our model achieves competitive performance against frontier models such as GPT-5. Ablation studies show that removing knowledge transfer reduces performance by 41 percent, while cache-aware rewards contribute a 17 percent improvement. Interestingly, reinforcement learning improves training stability but yields limited gains beyond strong supervised fine-tuning, suggesting that data quality and reward design play a more important role than complex optimization methods in building practical small agent models.

摘要：我們提出了CacheRL，一個用於訓練小型代理基礎模型的系統，在多步驟工具調用任務中達到92%的過程準確率，接近GPT-5的94%，同時所需計算量減少100倍。我們的方法解決了實際代理訓練中的三個挑戰：從大型模型中大規模轉移工具調用知識、在不需要昂貴的實時工具執行的情況下啟用強化學習，以及從噪聲緩存環境中穩健學習。CacheRL引入了三個關鍵創新。首先，一個混合思維軌跡管道通過LLM生成的推理痕跡增強代理軌跡，生成的訓練示例不僅教會模型調用哪些工具，還教會為什麼要這樣做。其次，CacheAgentLoop通過三層模糊緩存消除了實時執行成本，同時使用令牌級掩碼保持軌跡的真實性。第三，緩存層感知的獎勵動態調整答案質量權重，以避免因緩存引起的限制而懲罰模型。通過迭代的監督微調（SFT）和群體相對策略優化（GRPO），CacheRL將Qwen3-4B-Thinking的驗證獎勵從0.43提高到0.78。在公共代理工具調用基準上，我們的模型在與前沿模型如GPT-5的競爭中表現出色。消融研究表明，移除知識轉移會使性能降低41%，而緩存感知獎勵則貢獻了17%的改進。有趣的是，強化學習提高了訓練穩定性，但在強監督微調之外的收益有限，這表明數據質量和獎勵設計在構建實用的小型代理模型中比複雜的優化方法更為重要。

##### **VeriGeo: Controllable Geometry Question Generation with Numerical and Analytical Verification**
2606.14176v1 by Xiaoxian Duan, Zequn Liu, Yingce Xia

Geometry problem generation is useful for AI-assisted education and multimodal mathematical reasoning, but reliable synthesis remains difficult because the problem statement, diagram, constraints, and solution should be mutually consistent. Existing methods often trade off controllability and reliability: seed-based rewriting is flexible but weakly verifiable, whereas diagram-first construction improves validity but is less suited to arbitrary user-specified constraints. We introduce VeriGeo, a controllable geometry generation framework grounded in executable reasoning traces. Given user constraints such as target concepts and difficulty, an Author agent generates a problem and diagram, and a Solver agent produces a proof-aligned solution. Both agents use a shared action sequence that connects natural language, diagrams, geometric constraints, and proof steps into a verifiable representation. A three-stage pipeline checks numerical consistency, analytical realizability, and global consistency, using verification-guided reflection to repair recoverable failures and reject unrecoverable ones. Across five LLM backbones, raw generations frequently fail these checks, while VeriGeo repairs a substantial fraction of the invalid attempts. Supervised fine-tuning on 8.7k examples generated by VeriGeo achieves the best reported GeoQA performance among end-to-end multimodal LLM-based solvers, and obtains strong results on PGPS9K and MathVista-GPS, demonstrating the effectiveness of verified synthetic data for improving multimodal geometry reasoning.

摘要：幾何問題生成對於 AI 輔助教育和多模態數學推理非常有用，但由於問題陳述、圖示、約束和解決方案應該相互一致，因此可靠的合成仍然困難。現有的方法往往在可控性和可靠性之間進行取捨：基於種子的重寫靈活但驗證性較弱，而圖示優先的構建提高了有效性，但不太適合任意用戶指定的約束。我們介紹了 VeriGeo，一個基於可執行推理痕跡的可控幾何生成框架。根據用戶約束，如目標概念和難度，一個作者代理生成問題和圖示，而一個解決者代理則產生與證明對齊的解決方案。兩個代理使用共享的行動序列，將自然語言、圖示、幾何約束和證明步驟連接成可驗證的表示。一個三階段的管道檢查數值一致性、分析可實現性和全局一致性，使用驗證引導的反思來修復可恢復的失敗並拒絕不可恢復的失敗。在五個 LLM 主幹上，原始生成經常無法通過這些檢查，而 VeriGeo 修復了相當一部分無效的嘗試。對 VeriGeo 生成的 8.7k 範例進行的監督微調在端到端多模態 LLM 基礎的解決者中達到了最佳報告的 GeoQA 性能，並在 PGPS9K 和 MathVista-GPS 上取得了良好的結果，展示了經過驗證的合成數據在改善多模態幾何推理方面的有效性。

##### **Learning Urban Access Costs from Origin-Destination Flows via Inverse Optimal Transport**
2606.14157v1 by Paula Joy B. Martinez

Cities deliver basic services through mixed public-private facility networks, including schools, clinics, transit providers, and subsidized service points. In these systems, planners often observe where households go, but not the latent cost function through which they trade off factors such as distance, price, and institutional access. We study this urban problem through school choice in the Philippines, where the country's largest national education subsidy is intended to redirect learners from congested public schools to participating private schools. Treating school-to-school enrollment flows as an entropic optimal transport plan, we recover latent choice costs using two complementary inverse optimal transport models: an interpretable distance-banded model with a subsidy term, and a neural cost model trained through a differentiable Sinkhorn forward pass. Applied to 283{,}016 learner trips across 23{,}820 observed flows in the most populated region, the framework estimates a subsidy-equivalent distance, $λ^{(k)}$, interpreted as the kilometers of perceived travel cost offset by the subsidy. The case demonstrates how administrative origin-destination data can be transformed into interpretable planning metrics for accessibility-aware subsidy design, facility siting, and urban service allocation.

摘要：城市透過混合的公私設施網絡提供基本服務，包括學校、診所、交通提供者和補貼服務點。在這些系統中，規劃者通常觀察家庭的去向，但並不瞭解它們在距離、價格和機構可及性等因素之間權衡的潛在成本函數。我們通過菲律賓的學校選擇研究這一城市問題，該國最大的國家教育補貼旨在將學習者從擁擠的公立學校引導到參與的私立學校。將學校之間的入學流視為一種熵最優運輸計劃，我們使用兩個互補的逆最優運輸模型恢復潛在的選擇成本：一個可解釋的距離帶模型，帶有補貼項，以及一個通過可微分的Sinkhorn前向傳遞訓練的神經成本模型。應用於最人口稠密地區的283,016次學習者出行，涵蓋23,820個觀察流，該框架估算出一個補貼等效距離$λ^{(k)}$，該距離被解釋為補貼抵消的感知旅行成本的公里數。這一案例展示了如何將行政來源-目的地數據轉化為可解釋的規劃指標，以便進行考慮可及性的補貼設計、設施選址和城市服務分配。

##### **Graph-based Target Back-Propagation for Context Adaptation in Multi-LLM Agentic Systems**
2606.14155v1 by Tan Zhu, Tong Yao, Kananart Kuwaranancharoen, Amit Singh, Yushang Lai, Deepa Mohan, Shankara Bhargava

Context adaptation automates prompt engineering in LLM-based systems by iteratively revising tunable prompts from task feedback, without modifying model weights. Extending this paradigm to multi-LLM agentic systems is crucial: existing methods suffer from inaccurate credit assignment and lack convergence guarantees. We propose \textbf{G}raph-based \textbf{T}arget \textbf{B}ack-\textbf{P}ropagation (GTBP), a context adaptation framework for agentic workflows modeled as directed acyclic graphs. GTBP propagates local target outputs backward through the workflow graph and uses target--output discrepancies to guide a stage-wise prompt update mechanism. Theoretically, we show that GTBP's stage-wise prompt updates become stable over iterations, and that a sufficiently capable LLM optimizer can decrease the overall objective. Empirically, GTBP consistently outperforms strong baselines across three benchmarks while maintaining comparable computational cost.

摘要：上下文適應透過從任務反饋中反覆修訂可調整的提示，自動化了基於LLM的系統中的提示工程，而無需修改模型權重。將這一範式擴展到多LLM代理系統至關重要：現有方法存在不準確的信用分配和缺乏收斂保證的問題。我們提出了\textbf{G}raph-based \textbf{T}arget \textbf{B}ack-\textbf{P}ropagation (GTBP)，這是一個針對建模為有向無環圖的代理工作流程的上下文適應框架。GTBP通過工作流程圖向後傳播局部目標輸出，並利用目標與輸出之間的差異來指導分階段的提示更新機制。在理論上，我們表明GTBP的分階段提示更新在迭代過程中變得穩定，且一個足夠強大的LLM優化器可以降低整體目標。在實證上，GTBP在三個基準測試中始終優於強基線，同時保持可比的計算成本。

##### **Small LLMs: Pruning vs. Training from Scratch**
2606.14150v1 by Yufeng Xu, Taiming Lu, Kunjun Li, Jiachen Zhu, Mingjie Sun, Zhuang Liu

Pruning promises a shortcut to strong small language models. In this work, we examine this promise by pruning Llama-3.1-8B at pruning ratios of 0.5--0.8 with six methods spanning depth, width, and sparse granularities, under two controlled token-matched settings. (1) With the same training token budget, pruned initialization consistently outperforms random initialization. This shows that the parent model provides a strong starting point, although the advantage narrows as the training token budget grows and as the pruning ratio rises, nearly vanishing at the highest pruning ratio we study. (2) When training from scratch is instead given the full token budget consumed by the whole pipeline, pruning at finer granularities still retains an advantage, while coarser structured pruning can be matched or surpassed. This suggests that the parent model transfers knowledge that additional training tokens alone cannot fully recover, but only at fine granularity. Taken together, our results yield a clear recommendation: with a large pretrained model in hand and a limited training token budget, pruning is better than training from scratch; when the training budget is not limited, training from scratch can be competitive for coarser pruning, so a large pretrained parent is not always necessary.

摘要：修剪為強大的小型語言模型提供了一條捷徑。在這項工作中，我們通過以0.5至0.8的修剪比率修剪Llama-3.1-8B，並在兩個受控的標記匹配設置下，檢驗這一承諾，使用了六種涵蓋深度、寬度和稀疏粒度的方法。<lb/>（1）在相同的訓練標記預算下，修剪初始化始終優於隨機初始化。這顯示出母模型提供了一個強有力的起點，儘管隨著訓練標記預算的增長和修剪比率的上升，這一優勢會縮小，並在我們研究的最高修剪比率下幾乎消失。<lb/>（2）當從頭開始訓練時，則給予整個流程消耗的完整標記預算，修剪在更細的粒度下仍然保持優勢，而粗糙的結構化修剪可以被匹配或超越。這表明母模型轉移的知識是額外的訓練標記無法完全恢復的，但僅在細粒度下才能實現。<lb/>綜合來看，我們的結果提供了一個明確的建議：在手中擁有一個大型預訓練模型並且訓練標記預算有限的情況下，修剪比從頭開始訓練更好；當訓練預算不受限制時，從頭開始訓練在粗糙修剪上可以具有競爭力，因此大型預訓練母模型並不總是必要的。

##### **Personal Care Utility: Health as Everyday Infrastructure**
2606.14145v1 by Mahyar Abbasian, Elahe Khatibi, Saba A. Farahani, Nitish Nagesh, Arshia Ilaty, Hooman Sajjadi, Amir Rahmani, Ramesh Jain

Healthcare is essential, expert, and episodic by design - built around the roughly one hour per year a person spends with a clinician. The 8,759 hours outside clinical settings, where eating, sleeping, movement, medication, and stress actually shape long-term health, have no comparable infrastructure. The bottleneck for personalized health is not raw data or reasoning capability; it is the absence of that infrastructure layer. This paper introduces the Personal Care Utility (PCU): a layered, event-driven architecture proposed as the missing utility for everyday health, in the way that payments, networks, and power are utilities for their domains. PCU organizes continuous personal signals into semantically meaningful life events through a Personicle, estimates dynamic health state against personal baselines, reasons about cause and context, and routes guidance through an orchestrator that separates clinical decision logic, behavioral strategy selection, and natural-language expression. This separation lets large language models support reasoning and communication while keeping safety-critical clinical decisions grounded in validated evidence. We instantiate PCU for Type 2 Diabetes - turning CGM, meal, activity, medication, sleep, stress, and clinical data into glycemic events, individualized state estimates, causal explanations, and knowledge-grounded interventions. A day-in-the-life scenario shows the same infrastructure producing real-time nudges, weekly summaries, medication check-ins, silence, or deterministic safety alerts depending on context and risk. We close with how PCU generalizes to other chronic conditions and the governance questions any always-on personal health utility must address. The result is a blueprint that treats personalization not as a final messaging layer, but as an architectural property of everyday health guidance.

摘要：醫療保健是必不可少的、專業的，並且是按設計進行的——圍繞著一個人每年與臨床醫生相處的大約一小時。 在臨床環境之外的 8,759 小時中，飲食、睡眠、運動、用藥和壓力實際上塑造了長期健康，卻沒有相應的基礎設施。 個性化健康的瓶頸不是原始數據或推理能力，而是缺乏那一層基礎設施。 本文介紹了個人護理效用（PCU）：一種分層的、事件驅動的架構，作為日常健康的缺失效用，正如支付、網絡和電力是其領域的效用。 PCU 通過 Personicle 將持續的個人信號組織成語義上有意義的生活事件，根據個人基準估算動態健康狀態，推理原因和背景，並通過一個協調者路由指導，該協調者將臨床決策邏輯、行為策略選擇和自然語言表達分開。 這種分離使大型語言模型能夠支持推理和交流，同時使安全關鍵的臨床決策基於經過驗證的證據。 我們為 2 型糖尿病實現了 PCU——將 CGM、餐飲、活動、用藥、睡眠、壓力和臨床數據轉化為血糖事件、個性化狀態估算、因果解釋和基於知識的干預。 一個日常生活場景顯示相同的基礎設施根據上下文和風險產生實時提示、每週摘要、用藥檢查、靜默或確定性安全警報。 我們最後討論 PCU 如何推廣到其他慢性病以及任何始終在線的個人健康效用必須解決的治理問題。 最終結果是一個藍圖，將個性化視為日常健康指導的架構特性，而不是最終的消息層。

##### **Implicit Reasoning for Large Language Model-based Generative Recommendation**
2606.14142v1 by Yinhan He, Liam Collins, Bhuvesh Kumar, Jundong Li, Neil Shah, Donald Loveland

Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly adopted as backbones for Generative Recommendation (GR), promising access to pretrained world knowledge. Yet reliably invoking this knowledge for GR remains poorly understood. A key obstacle is that LLM-based GR typically represents items with Semantic IDs (SIDs), disrupting LLMs' natural-language reasoning interface because these tokens are unseen by the LLM during pretraining. Existing approaches address this with expensive multi-stage pipelines that ground SIDs and elicit explicit rationales, but offer limited insight into when and why each stage is necessary. In this work, we systematically decompose explicit reasoning training pipelines for LLM-based GR, revealing three key limitations: weakened world-knowledge verbalization, misalignment between SID and natural-language token embedding spaces, and sensitivity to rationale quality, all of which hurt explicit reasoning performance. To circumvent these issues, we propose PauseRec, a lightweight implicit reasoning paradigm tailored for GR. PauseRec is exceptionally practical, avoiding costly reasoning trace acquisition and reasoning alignment training, leading to a multitude of benefits: (1) it outperforms standard explicit CoT methods by up to 6.22%, (2) it reduces training cost by up to 65% GPU hours, and (3) it speeds up inference by up to 71.3%. These results position PauseRec as a lightweight alternative to explicit rationale generation, enabling more effective and efficient LLM-based GR.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地被用作生成推薦（GR）的基礎，承諾能夠訪問預訓練的世界知識。<lb/>然而，可靠地調用這些知識以進行GR仍然不甚明瞭。<lb/>一個主要障礙是基於LLM的GR通常使用語義ID（SIDs）來表示項目，這破壞了LLM的自然語言推理介面，因為這些標記在預訓練期間對LLM來說是不可見的。<lb/>現有的方法通過昂貴的多階段管道來解決這個問題，這些管道將SIDs與明確的推理聯繫起來，但對於每個階段何時以及為何必要的見解有限。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們系統性地分解了基於LLM的GR的明確推理訓練管道，揭示了三個主要限制：削弱的世界知識口述、SID與自然語言標記嵌入空間之間的不對齊，以及對推理質量的敏感性，這些都損害了明確推理的性能。<lb/>為了迴避這些問題，我們提出了PauseRec，一種針對GR量身定制的輕量級隱式推理範式。<lb/>PauseRec在實用性上表現出色，避免了昂貴的推理追蹤獲取和推理對齊訓練，帶來了多重好處：（1）它的表現超過標準的明確CoT方法，最多可達6.22%；（2）它將訓練成本降低了最多65%的GPU小時；（3）它的推理速度提高了最多71.3%。<lb/>這些結果使PauseRec成為明確推理生成的輕量級替代方案，從而實現更有效和高效的基於LLM的GR。

##### **Spatio-Temporal Audio Language Modeling for Dynamic Sound Sources**
2606.14141v1 by Oh Hyun-Bin, Kazuki Shimada, Yuhta Takida, Kim Sung-Bin, Toshimitsu Uesaka, Takashi Shibuya, Kyeongyoon Lee, Tae-Hyun Oh, Yuki Mitsufuji

Sound events are entities with semantic identities, locations, and trajectories, but current audio-language models usually reason about clips as global event content. Conversely, sound event localization models track source directions over time but offer limited semantic coverage for language reasoning. To address this gap, we introduce ST-AudioQA, a spatio-temporal audio QA dataset and benchmark built from first-order ambisonic (FOA) renderings of static and moving sound sources. Each scene provides source identity, activity, direction, distance, and motion metadata, enabling dense trajectory supervision and questions about what is sounding, where it is, how it moves, and how sources relate. We further propose ST-Audio Encoder, a time-resolved FOA audio encoder that learns event semantics together with source trajectories, and ST-AudioLM, which connects the audio tokens from the encoder to an LLM for spatio-temporal audio QA. Experiments show that this representation improves the semantic-localization tradeoff and yields stronger reasoning performance than static spatial and localization-oriented baselines.

摘要：聲音事件是具有語義身份、位置和軌跡的實體，但當前的音頻語言模型通常將片段視為全球事件內容。相反，聲音事件定位模型隨時間跟踪來源方向，但對語言推理的語義覆蓋有限。為了解決這一空白，我們引入了ST-AudioQA，一個基於靜態和移動聲音源的一階環繞聲（FOA）渲染構建的時空音頻問答數據集和基準。每個場景提供來源身份、活動、方向、距離和運動元數據，從而實現密集的軌跡監督以及關於聲音來源、位置、運動方式和來源之間關係的問題。我們進一步提出了ST-Audio Encoder，一個時間解析的FOA音頻編碼器，能夠學習事件語義以及來源軌跡，還有ST-AudioLM，將編碼器的音頻標記與大型語言模型（LLM）連接，用於時空音頻問答。實驗表明，這種表示改善了語義與定位之間的權衡，並且比靜態空間和定位導向的基準表現出更強的推理性能。

##### **CoRe: A Continuously Reward-Finetuned LLM Query Rewriter for Multi-Stage Context-Aware Relevance in Web-Scale Video Search**
2606.14127v1 by Yilin Wen, Rong Yang, Xiaojia Chang, Hong Sun, Gefu Tang, Chunhui Liu, Jeffrey Chen, Zeyu Ma, Lisong Qiu, Xiaochuan Fan, Congjia Yu, Quan Zhou, Yuheng Chen, Zian Wang

LLM-based query rewriters in production face a tension: the training reward must reflect how the rewrite is consumed by the production ranker, yet the training procedure must be cheap enough to support continuous redeployment as data drifts. We present CoRe (Context Relevance), such a system, redeployed weekly for over five months in a major short-video search engine. Our reward uses the deployed multimodal relevance model as its source and a multiplicative ratio form mirroring the production fusion algebra, closing the simulation-production gap that offline reward proxies leave open. A semi-online Mixed Preference Optimization loop makes this reward affordable at multi-million-instance weekly scale: a DPO-style pairwise objective restricts the gradient pass to a small top-k/bottom-k subset of sampled trajectories, and a phase structure reduces trainer/inference-server parameter syncs from per-step to per-phase. An automated promotion gate over reward-like and stability metrics detected and recovered from a real reward-hacking incident in production. Rewriter output is consumed as parallel relevance signals at recall, rawrank, and finerank without displacing the original signals, bounding rewriter-failure blast radius. Online A/B from two sequential production launches, first deploying the rewriter at finerank, then extending consumption to recall and rawrank, delivers statistically significant reductions in change-query rate on rewrite-impacted queries, with all headline relevance and engagement metrics moving in the expected direction.

摘要：LLM 基於查詢重寫器在生產中面臨著一種緊張關係：訓練獎勵必須反映重寫如何被生產排名器消耗，但訓練過程必須足夠便宜，以支持隨著數據漂移的持續重新部署。我們提出了 CoRe（上下文相關性），這是一個系統，在一個主要的短視頻搜索引擎中每週重新部署超過五個月。我們的獎勵使用已部署的多模態相關性模型作為其來源，並以乘法比率形式反映生產融合代數，縮小了離線獎勵代理留下的模擬-生產差距。一個半在線的混合偏好優化循環使得這個獎勵在每週數百萬實例的規模上變得可負擔：一個 DPO 風格的成對目標將梯度傳遞限制在一小部分 top-k/bottom-k 的抽樣軌跡中，並且一個階段結構將訓練者/推理伺服器的參數同步從每步減少到每階段。自動化的促銷閘門通過類似獎勵和穩定性指標檢測並從生產中的一次真實獎勵黑客事件中恢復。重寫器的輸出在召回、原始排名和精細排名中作為平行相關信號被消耗，而不會取代原始信號，限制了重寫器失敗的爆炸半徑。來自兩次連續生產發布的在線 A/B 測試，首次在精細排名中部署重寫器，然後將消耗擴展到召回和原始排名，顯示在重寫影響的查詢上，變更查詢率顯著降低，所有標題相關性和參與指標均朝著預期方向移動。

##### **Recovering Stranded Discrimination in Knowledge Tracing: Per-Item Bias Correction via Empirical-Bayes Shrinkage**
2606.14123v1 by Xiaoran Yan, Cheng Tang, Atsushi Shimada

Deployed knowledge-tracing models are typically frozen after training, yet systematic per-item logit bias arises, from limited per-item expressivity in backbone architectures and from post-deployment shifts in item properties, degrading prediction quality. Global post-hoc calibrators such as Platt scaling, temperature scaling, and isotonic regression improve probability estimates but leave discriminative ability, as measured by AUC, unchanged. This AUC invariance is a structural consequence of monotone score-only transforms; recovering the stranded discrimination requires conditioning on item identity. We propose SLC (State-space Logit Correction), which converts binary observations to Gaussian pseudo-observations via Laplace/IRLS, applies empirical-Bayes shrinkage through a Kalman smoother, and fits an offset-Platt link. The state-space formulation also yields a detectability bound that characterizes the Bernoulli information floor, explaining why temporal tracking provides no benefit at current data densities. Across four datasets, five backbones, and three seeds, SLC improves AUC on all four datasets and NLL on three, with the advantage concentrating on sparse items. Cross-domain controls suggest that the same phenomenon can arise beyond education when the deployed backbone leaves entity-level bias.

摘要：已部署的知識追蹤模型在訓練後通常會被凍結，但由於主幹架構中每個項目的表達能力有限，以及部署後項目屬性的變化，導致系統性的每項邏輯偏差，從而降低預測質量。全球事後校準器如 Platt 標定、溫度標定和等距回歸改善了概率估計，但對於 AUC 測量的區分能力則沒有改變。這種 AUC 不變性是單調分數轉換的結構性結果；恢復被孤立的區分能力需要對項目身份進行條件化。我們提出了 SLC（狀態空間邏輯校正），通過 Laplace/IRLS 將二元觀察轉換為高斯偽觀察，通過卡爾曼平滑器應用經驗貝葉斯收縮，並擬合偏移 Platt 連結。狀態空間的公式還產生了一個可檢測性界限，描述了伯努利信息底線，解釋了為什麼在當前數據密度下，時間追蹤沒有提供任何好處。在四個數據集、五個主幹和三個隨機種子中，SLC 在所有四個數據集上改善了 AUC，在三個數據集上改善了 NLL，且優勢集中在稀疏項目上。跨領域的控制表明，當部署的主幹留下實體級別的偏差時，這種現象也可能在教育之外出現。

##### **Beyond Perplexity: UTF-8 Validity in Byte-aware Language Models**
2606.14122v1 by Sangwhan Moon, Daisuke Oba, Youmi Ma, Tatsuya Hiraoka, Naoaki Okazaki

Byte-level tokenization enables language models to handle any Unicode input, but models can generate invalid UTF-8 sequences when encountering rare or unseen characters. We investigate the relationship between training scale and UTF-8 generation reliability with a 355M parameter model trained on 80B tokens from a balanced multilingual corpus of English, Japanese, Korean, and Chinese. We introduce multiple evaluation protocols that isolate UTF-8 structural validity from language modeling. UTF-8 validity convergence lags perplexity by a roughly a factor of two: perplexity stabilizes after 2.1B tokens, but UTF-8 validity requires 4.2B tokens. In context-free generation, rare characters achieve higher structural validity than common characters, suggesting over-specialization of frequent character representations. Through experiments, we observed that reliable UTF-8 generation is a distinct capability requiring evaluation beyond perplexity.

摘要：字節級的標記化使語言模型能夠處理任何 Unicode 輸入，但當遇到罕見或未見過的字符時，模型可能會生成無效的 UTF-8 序列。我們調查了訓練規模與 UTF-8 生成可靠性之間的關係，使用一個 355M 參數的模型，該模型在來自平衡多語言語料庫的 80B 令牌上進行訓練，語言包括英語、日語、韓語和中文。我們引入了多個評估協議，以隔離 UTF-8 結構有效性與語言建模之間的關係。UTF-8 有效性收斂的速度大約比困惑度慢兩倍：困惑度在 2.1B 令牌後穩定，但 UTF-8 有效性需要 4.2B 令牌。在無上下文生成中，罕見字符的結構有效性高於常見字符，這表明頻繁字符表示的過度專門化。通過實驗，我們觀察到可靠的 UTF-8 生成是一種獨特的能力，需要超越困惑度的評估。

##### **FAConformer: Frequency-Aware Convolutional Transformer for Auditory Attention Decoding**
2606.14120v1 by Ziwei Wang, Xingyi He, Tianwang Jia, Hongbin Wang, Dongrui Wu

Auditory attention decoding (AAD) aims to infer the attended speaker from neural responses in multi-speaker acoustic environments and is a key problem for neuro-steered hearing systems. Although recent studies have achieved encouraging progress, existing AAD models still do not fully exploit frequency domain electroencephalography (EEG) information. In particular, most approaches introduce multi-band information through handcrafted feature extraction or direct cross-band feature concatenation, which mainly exploit frequency information at a shallow level and may overlook band-specific patterns and cross-band interactions. To address these limitations, this paper proposes FAConformer, a frequency-aware CNN-Transformer framework for AAD that explicitly integrates band-specific encoding and adaptive cross-band interaction. Specifically, FAConformer first decomposes EEG signals into multiple frequency bands and assigns each band to an independent CNN-Transformer encoder for band-specific modeling. The resulting band-wise features are then adaptively fused by a carefully designed frequency-aware attention (FAA) module that models cross-band dependencies by treating band-wise features as tokens. Further, band-wise auxiliary supervision (BAS) is introduced to prevent weakly contributing branches from being under-optimized during joint training. In this way, FAConformer performs frequency-aware modeling that more effectively exploits frequency domain information. Extensive experiments on two public AAD datasets with three decision-window lengths demonstrated that FAConformer consistently outperformed 12 competitive baselines, surpassing the current state-of-the-art model by 4.9%. Further analyses of band importance, ablation, and parameter sensitivity verify the effectiveness, robustness, and interpretability of the proposed framework. Code is available at https://github.com/wzwvv/FAConformer.

摘要：聽覺注意解碼（AAD）旨在從多說話者的聲學環境中的神經反應推斷所關注的說話者，是神經導向聽力系統的一個關鍵問題。儘管最近的研究取得了令人鼓舞的進展，但現有的AAD模型仍未充分利用頻域腦電圖（EEG）信息。特別是，大多數方法通過手工特徵提取或直接的跨頻帶特徵串聯引入多頻帶信息，這主要是在淺層次上利用頻率信息，可能忽略了特定頻帶的模式和跨頻帶的交互。為了解決這些限制，本文提出了FAConformer，一種針對AAD的頻率感知CNN-Transformer框架，明確整合了特定頻帶編碼和自適應跨頻帶交互。具體來說，FAConformer首先將EEG信號分解為多個頻帶，並為每個頻帶分配一個獨立的CNN-Transformer編碼器以進行特定頻帶建模。隨後，通過精心設計的頻率感知注意（FAA）模塊，自適應地融合所得到的頻帶特徵，該模塊通過將頻帶特徵視為標記來建模跨頻帶的依賴性。此外，引入了頻帶輔助監督（BAS），以防止在聯合訓練期間貢獻較弱的分支被低估優化。這樣，FAConformer執行頻率感知建模，更有效地利用頻域信息。在兩個公共AAD數據集上進行的廣泛實驗，使用三個決策窗口長度，顯示FAConformer始終超越12個競爭基準，超過當前最先進的模型4.9%。對頻帶重要性、消融和參數敏感性的進一步分析驗證了所提框架的有效性、穩健性和可解釋性。代碼可在 https://github.com/wzwvv/FAConformer 獲得。

##### **FactoryLLM: A Safe and Open-Source AI Playground for Evaluating LLMs in Smart Factories**
2606.14119v1 by Yash Pulse, Yong-Bin Kang, Abhik Banerjee, Abdur Forkan, Prem Prakash Jayaraman

Fault diagnostics and recovery in smart factories is challenging because critical information is dispersed across manuals of multiple machines which are interconnected through the manufacturing process. Large Language Models (LLMs) can provide a promising approach. In this paper, we propose FactoryLLM, a safe and open-source AI playground designed for evaluating different LLM-based retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) models by analysing documents from multiple machines across the manufacturing process. FactoryLLM enables the user to configure the LLM, and assess performance when reasoning over multiple documents, through a dual evaluation setup using both RAGAS and NVIDIA's LLM-as-a-Judge metrics. FactoryLLM is safe because it allows users to run local or open-source LLMs without sharing sensitive industrial data, providing a controlled environment for experimentation. We demonstrate the efficacy of FactoryLLM through a case study which involves an Autonomous Intelligent Vehicle and its Mobile Planner software, evaluating three LLMs across 30 maintenance queries derived from approximately 600 pages of cross-machine documentation. The results suggest that FactoryLLM is effective in cross-machine document reasoning: every model achieved a groundedness score above 0.88. The full code and documentation for community to test FactoryLLM with their manufacturing specific scenarios are publicly available.

摘要：故障診斷和恢復在智慧工廠中具有挑戰性，因為關鍵資訊分散在多台機器的手冊中，這些機器通過製造過程互相連接。大型語言模型（LLMs）可以提供一種有前景的方法。在本文中，我們提出了FactoryLLM，這是一個安全且開源的AI遊樂場，旨在通過分析來自製造過程中多台機器的文件來評估不同基於LLM的檢索增強生成（RAG）模型。FactoryLLM使使用者能夠配置LLM，並在多文件推理時評估性能，通過使用RAGAS和NVIDIA的LLM-as-a-Judge指標的雙重評估設置。FactoryLLM是安全的，因為它允許用戶運行本地或開源的LLM，而無需共享敏感的工業數據，提供了一個受控的實驗環境。我們通過一個案例研究展示了FactoryLLM的有效性，該研究涉及一個自主智能車輛及其移動規劃軟體，評估了三個LLM在大約600頁跨機器文檔中衍生的30個維護查詢的表現。結果表明，FactoryLLM在跨機器文檔推理方面是有效的：每個模型的基礎分數均超過0.88。完整的代碼和文檔可供社區在其特定製造場景中測試FactoryLLM，並已公開提供。

##### **A Two-Stage Statistical Framework for Evaluating Associative Interference in Large Language Models**
2606.14117v1 by Achraf Cohen, Andrew Kincaid

Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly evaluated for bias using adaptations of human psychological paradigms, yet methodological limitations-particularly the conflation of refusal behavior with task performance-have hindered clear interpretation. Here, we adapt the Implicit Association Test (IAT) to a controlled, forced-choice framework and introduce a two-stage modeling approach that separates response compliance from task-consistent classification. Across three contemporary LLMs (Claude Sonnet-4, Gemini 2.5 Pro, and GPT-5), we evaluate associative interference, defined as reduced task-consistency in incongruent relative to congruent conditions. While compliance with the structured response format was uniformly high, interference effects varied substantially across models and domains. Claude Sonnet-4 exhibited strong interference in the Gender--Career domain (DeltaP = 0.086, 95% CrI [0.026, 0.173]) and smaller but credible effects in Gender--Science. Gemini 2.5 Pro showed attenuated interference, and GPT-5 exhibited minimal or no detectable interference across domains. These findings demonstrate that IAT-style associative asymmetries are not a universal property of LLMs, but instead depend on model-specific characteristics. By isolating interference from compliance and modeling item-level variability, this study provides a principled framework for evaluating structured response patterns in LLMs. The results highlight the importance of model-specific assessment and suggest that associative interference can be substantially mitigated in modern systems.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）越來越多地使用人類心理學範式的改編來評估偏見，然而方法論的限制——特別是將拒絕行為與任務表現混為一談——阻礙了清晰的解釋。在這裡，我們將隱性聯想測試（IAT）調整為一個受控的強制選擇框架，並引入一種兩階段建模方法，將響應合規性與任務一致性分類分開。在三個當代LLM（Claude Sonnet-4、Gemini 2.5 Pro 和 GPT-5）中，我們評估了聯想干擾，定義為在不一致條件下的任務一致性降低，相對於一致條件。儘管對結構化響應格式的合規性普遍較高，但干擾效應在模型和領域之間變化顯著。Claude Sonnet-4 在性別-職業領域顯示出強烈的干擾（DeltaP = 0.086, 95% CrI [0.026, 0.173]），在性別-科學上則顯示出較小但可信的效應。Gemini 2.5 Pro 顯示出減弱的干擾，而 GPT-5 在各個領域中幾乎沒有或無法檢測到干擾。這些發現表明，IAT風格的聯想不對稱並不是LLM的普遍特性，而是依賴於模型特定的特徵。通過將干擾與合規性隔離並建模項目級變異性，本研究提供了一個原則性框架，用於評估LLM中的結構化響應模式。結果突顯了模型特定評估的重要性，並表明聯想干擾在現代系統中可以顯著減輕。

##### **Simulating Students' Java Programming Errors with Large Language Models**
2606.14113v1 by Ali Keramati, Jie Cao, Iman Mohammadi, Mark Warschauer, Yang Shi

Understanding student errors in the programming is a cornerstone of programming education, yet obtaining a representative set of student errors for any newly designed task remains slow and costly, since authentic submissions only accumulate after extensive classroom deployment. This paper explores whether large language models (LLMs) can serve as scalable proxies for students by simulating realistic logical errors in code submissions. Using the CodeWorkout dataset of 74,000+ unique student Java submissions across 37 problems, we evaluate five LLMs under three mainstream prompting strategies: Input-Output (IO), Chain-of-Thought (CoT), and iterative Self-Refine. We assess performance along two key dimensions: diversity (the range of distinct error patterns) and alignment (alignment with authentic student mistakes), and examine how these vary by struggling level of programming tasks. Our quantitative findings reveal that while all models generate diverse errors, their alignment to human submissions diverges: Claude Sonnet 4 achieves the most balanced performance. In addition, we conducted a blinded expert annotation study (N = 401) comparing synthetic and authentic errors. This qualitative analysis confirms that the generated errors are functionally indistinguishable from authentic student errors. Moreover, higher-struggling-level problems elicit more diverse but less student-like errors. These results highlight trade-offs in using LLMs to simulate human learners and suggest design considerations for integrating synthetic errors into teachable agents, intelligent tutoring systems, and large-scale learning analytics.

摘要：理解學生在程式設計中的錯誤是程式教育的基石，然而獲得任何新設計任務的代表性學生錯誤集仍然緩慢且昂貴，因為真實的提交只有在廣泛的課堂部署後才能累積。本文探討大型語言模型（LLMs）是否可以作為學生的可擴展代理，通過模擬程式提交中的現實邏輯錯誤來實現。利用 CodeWorkout 數據集中的 74,000 多個獨特學生 Java 提交，涵蓋 37 個問題，我們在三種主流提示策略下評估五個 LLM：輸入-輸出（IO）、思維鏈（CoT）和迭代自我精煉。我們從兩個關鍵維度評估性能：多樣性（不同錯誤模式的範圍）和一致性（與真實學生錯誤的一致性），並檢查這些如何因程式任務的困難程度而異。我們的定量研究結果顯示，雖然所有模型都生成多樣的錯誤，但它們與人類提交的一致性卻有所不同：Claude Sonnet 4 實現了最平衡的表現。此外，我們進行了一項盲測專家註釋研究（N = 401），比較合成錯誤和真實錯誤。這項定性分析確認生成的錯誤在功能上與真實學生錯誤無法區分。此外，更高困難程度的問題引發了更多樣但不那麼類似學生的錯誤。這些結果突顯了使用 LLM 模擬人類學習者的權衡，並提出了將合成錯誤整合到可教代理、智能輔導系統和大規模學習分析中的設計考量。

##### **Numbers Already Carry Their Own Embeddings**
2606.14108v1 by Suhyun Bae, Donghun Lee

We introduce Adelic operation-preserved embeddings (AOE), a training-free representation that captures both a number's real value and its modular (p-adic) signatures. This construction preserves additive and multiplicative structure by design, turning numerical input into embeddings that "speak in the language of mathematics." Unlike prior approaches that rely on task-specific retraining, AOE is plug-and-play and drops seamlessly into existing architectures. On algebraic combinatorics benchmarks, it delivers consistent gains including the first-ever perfect accuracy on the Weaving Pattern task-while suggesting a principled path forward for overcoming the long-standing "number problem" in AI.

摘要：我們介紹了保留運算的 Adelic 嵌入 (AOE)，這是一種無需訓練的表示法，能夠捕捉數字的實際值及其模 (p-adic) 簽名。這一構造通過設計保留了加法和乘法結構，將數值輸入轉換為「用數學語言表達」的嵌入。與依賴於特定任務重新訓練的先前方法不同，AOE 是即插即用的，能夠無縫融入現有架構。在代數組合數學基準測試中，它提供了一致的增益，包括在編織模式任務上首次實現完美準確率，同時為克服 AI 中長期存在的「數字問題」提供了一條有原則的前進道路。

##### **Clay-CNN Hybrids: Leveraging Geo-Foundational Models as Auxiliary Context for Landslide Detection**
2606.14081v1 by Huong Binh Vu

Rapid post-event landslide mapping is essential for disaster response but remains difficult to automate due to extreme class imbalance. This study evaluates whether Clay v1.5, a Geo-Foundational Model (GFM), can improve pixel-level landslide segmentation on the Landslide4Sense (L4S) benchmark, which contains 3,799 training chips with 14 Sentinel-2 and terrain bands and approximately 2% positive pixels. We compare three strategies: Clay as the primary encoder with multi-scale residual terrain fusion, a U-Net backbone augmented with Clay semantic context at the bottleneck, and a standard U-Net baseline. The hybrid U-Net + Clay model with two-stage Low-Rank Adaptation (LoRA) achieved the best test F1 of 64.5 +/- 1.8% over three seeds, surpassing the Clay-only backbone (55.2 +/- 3.6%) and the U-Net baseline (59.9%). Clay as a standalone encoder underperformed the U-Net due to the absence of multi-scale skip connections, but its pretrained representations consistently improved performance when injected as auxiliary context. These findings suggest that GFMs are most effective for landslide detection when they complement spatially detailed convolutional architectures rather than replace them.

摘要：快速的事件後滑坡映射對於災害應對至關重要，但由於極端的類別不平衡，仍然難以自動化。本研究評估了 Geo-Foundational Model (GFM) Clay v1.5 是否能改善 Landslide4Sense (L4S) 基準上的像素級滑坡分割，該基準包含 3,799 個訓練樣本，擁有 14 個 Sentinel-2 和地形波段，正樣本約佔 2%。我們比較了三種策略：將 Clay 作為主要編碼器，結合多尺度殘差地形融合；一個 U-Net 骨幹，在瓶頸處增強 Clay 語義上下文；以及一個標準的 U-Net 基準。使用兩階段低秩適應 (LoRA) 的混合 U-Net + Clay 模型在三個隨機種子上達到了最佳測試 F1 值 64.5 +/- 1.8%，超過了僅使用 Clay 的骨幹 (55.2 +/- 3.6%) 和 U-Net 基準 (59.9%)。作為獨立編碼器的 Clay 表現不如 U-Net，因為缺乏多尺度跳躍連接，但當作為輔助上下文注入時，其預訓練表示始終改善了性能。這些發現表明，GFM 在滑坡檢測中最有效的方式是補充空間詳細的卷積架構，而不是取而代之。

##### **Rethinking Backdoor Adversarial Unlearning through the Lens of Catastrophic Forgetting in Continual Learning**
2606.14078v1 by Zhenqian Zhu, Yamin Hu, Yujiang Liu, Luping Wei, Wenbo Hou, Bin Li, Haodong Li, Wenjian Luo

Existing studies reveal that current backdoor defenses exhibit limited robustness and often fail against specific types of attacks. More concerningly, prevailing safety tuning strategies tend to provide only superficial safety protection, as they fall short of completely eliminating the backdoor effects. In this work, we present a novel formulation of backdoor learning and unlearning as a sequential, three-stage process from a continual learning perspective. Within this framework, we formally define complete backdoor unlearning and further derive the necessary conditions for achieving it based on the mechanism of catastrophic forgetting. Guided by these insights, we propose Blind Inversion-Backdoor Adversarial Unlearning (BI-BAU), which formulates the generation of adversarial examples satisfying the unlearning conditions as a blind inversion problem. We solve this by integrating the bi-level optimization process of adversarial training into an Expectation-Maximization (EM) algorithm framework to optimize the maximum a posteriori (MAP) objective. Furthermore, BI-BAU is extended to untargeted adversarial scenarios with unknown target classes, as well as to multi-modal contrastive learning tasks, enhancing its applicability to real-world deployment scenarios where pre-trained models may be compromised. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method exhibits general applicability across a wide spectrum of backdoor attacks and can effectively and thoroughly eliminate the backdoor effects from a backdoor model.

摘要：現有研究顯示，目前的後門防禦展現出有限的穩健性，並且經常無法抵抗特定類型的攻擊。更令人擔憂的是，現行的安全調整策略往往僅提供表面的安全保護，因為它們無法完全消除後門效應。在這項工作中，我們從持續學習的角度提出了一種新的後門學習和去學習的公式，將其視為一個連續的三階段過程。在這個框架內，我們正式定義了完全的後門去學習，並進一步推導出基於災難性遺忘機制實現它所需的條件。在這些見解的指導下，我們提出了盲反轉後門對抗去學習（BI-BAU），將滿足去學習條件的對抗樣本生成公式化為一個盲反轉問題。我們通過將對抗訓練的雙層優化過程整合到期望最大化（EM）算法框架中來解決此問題，以優化最大後驗（MAP）目標。此外，BI-BAU 擴展到未知目標類別的無目標對抗場景，以及多模態對比學習任務，增強了其在現實世界部署場景中的適用性，特別是在預訓練模型可能受到攻擊的情況下。大量實驗表明，我們的方法在各種後門攻擊中展現出普遍的適用性，並能有效且徹底地消除後門模型中的後門效應。

##### **Diffusion-Refined Segmentation and Vision-Language Interpretation for Pediatric Brain Tumor MRI**
2606.14072v1 by Wentao Ke, Jianche Liu

Accurate pediatric brain tumor segmentation remains challenging due to limited annotated data, heterogeneous imaging phenotypes, diffuse tumor boundaries, and class imbalance across tumor subregions. Here, we present a two-stage deep learning framework for improving multi-modal pediatric brain MRI segmentation and clinical interpretation. First, we evaluate 3D Res U-Net and Swin-UNETR baselines on BraTS-PEDs MRI scans, using four co-registered modalities to predict tumor core, whole tumor, and enhancing tumor regions. Second, we introduce diffusion-based refinement models conditioned on coarse Swin-UNETR predictions, including a 3D DDPM refiner and MedSegDiff. Conditioning substantially improves diffusion stability and performance, particularly for enhancing tumor boundary segmentation. Conditioned MedSegDiff achieves the strongest boundary agreement with the lowest HD95. Finally, predicted tumor volumes and representative segmentation overlays are integrated with a multimodal language model to generate structured radiology-style reports. Together, our results suggest that coarse-to-refined diffusion segmentation can improve pediatric tumor boundary delineation and support end-to-end interpretable AI-assisted neuro-oncology workflows.

摘要：準確的兒科腦腫瘤分割仍然具有挑戰性，原因包括有限的標註數據、異質的影像表型、擴散的腫瘤邊界，以及腫瘤子區域之間的類別不平衡。<lb/>在此，我們提出了一個兩階段的深度學習框架，以改善多模態兒科腦部MRI的分割和臨床解釋。<lb/>首先，我們在BraTS-PEDs MRI掃描上評估3D Res U-Net和Swin-UNETR基準，使用四種共同註冊的模態來預測腫瘤核心、整體腫瘤和增強腫瘤區域。<lb/>其次，我們引入基於擴散的精煉模型，這些模型是以粗略的Swin-UNETR預測為條件，包括3D DDPM精煉器和MedSegDiff。<lb/>條件化顯著改善了擴散的穩定性和性能，特別是在增強腫瘤邊界分割方面。<lb/>條件化的MedSegDiff在邊界一致性方面達到了最強的表現，並且具有最低的HD95。<lb/>最後，預測的腫瘤體積和代表性的分割重疊圖與多模態語言模型集成，以生成結構化的放射學風格報告。<lb/>綜合來看，我們的結果表明，粗到精的擴散分割可以改善兒科腫瘤邊界的描繪，並支持端到端可解釋的AI輔助神經腫瘤學工作流程。
